Current Commentary

Roosevelt's Good Neighbor Policy and Hirota's Diplomacy

— Zhen

U.S. Secretary of State Hull previously gave a speech to the Canadian Council in New York. "President Roosevelt's Good Neighbor Policy is centered on relations with the Far East... It is quite similar to the Atlantic and Pacific issues. The method of agreed-upon meetings seeks political and economic stability, and the maintenance of peace through non-aggression and reduction of armaments." He also said, "There are also our territories and possessions on the vast Pacific Ocean... Such as the Open Door Policy, which has long been clearly stipulated by treaties... And it is a way to maintain peace in the Far East and the Pacific... Such as the Washington Treaty, which has been very effective... We still deeply believe in and abide by it..." Such a proposition is indeed based on the spirit of peace in its words. It reiterates that the United States' diplomacy towards the Far East should at least be given equal importance as its diplomacy towards Western Europe. Although its specific strategies are unknowable, its principles have been expressed without a doubt.

The United States has been pursuing the Monroe Doctrine for more than a century. In the past, it did not want to intervene in events outside the Americas and was also unable to do so. Therefore, the United States had no expression other than observation in the complex and complicated European issues. However, since the sudden outbreak of the European War in 1914, the national power of the United States has suddenly expanded. Its economic relations have expanded from South America to the countries of the European continent. During the war, the United States invested more than 10 billion U.S. dollars in European countries. All major European countries have close economic ties with the United States. However, after the war, European countries were exhausted. The situation of their mutual opposition and conflict is also very complicated. For more than ten years, the United States has only watched from the sidelines and has not taken any actions to resolve the difficulties. There are reasons for this. It is not necessarily all because it has been isolated for a long time and is not accustomed to international diplomacy.

The issue of war debt repayment is one of the stumbling blocks between Britain and the United States. At the same time, it also often causes unhappiness between the United States and France. Since the debt cannot be recovered, it is difficult to establish the economic prosperity of the United States. If the period of panic is prolonged, it will eventually lead to huge disasters that are difficult to resolve. For the sake of the United States, the only way to resolve the current difficulties is to find another market outside of Europe. There is one place. Although it is not enough to provide for the expansion of the United States in the short term, it is indeed very promising in the future, that is, the Far East. The international relations in the Far East are simpler than those in Western Europe, and it is an undeveloped area. It is not like Europe, where manufacturing industries have reached their peak. Even Japan, a country that claims to be gradually advancing to heavy industry, often imports about 200 million Japanese yen worth of steel machinery every year. The United States accounts for a major position in automobiles, machinery, and steel. Japan is like this, not to mention the other countries that can provide for the United States's unlimited development. This is why the United States must adhere to the Open Door Policy, in order to retain the Far East market and use it as a place for future economic development. However, first there is the lack of coordination between Britain and the United States in the Far East, followed by the opposition between Japan and the United States. Once the Soviet Union rises in Eastern Europe and is now extending its strategy to Siberia, the four powers of Britain, the United States, Japan, and the Soviet Union form a quadrilateral power. It is even more difficult for the United States to actively develop the East Asian market.

Japan has recently been advocating equality in armaments. The so-called equality in armaments does not mean that Germany wants to obtain the same strength as Britain and the United States in the army and air force. Japan's army can be called the first in the Far East, with no opponents. What it is fighting for is the equality of naval power. Since the abolition of the naval holiday, Japan has been preparing to build ships freely in two years, without being restricted by treaties. In other words, it will no longer be bound by the Washington Treaty.

However, the current Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota is still touting the slogan of "moral" diplomacy. He is singing peace with Britain, the United States, and the Soviet Union, as if he really wants to make the Pacific calm. We will not ask about the content of moral diplomacy, but will try to study the current situation in Japan. First, the democratic meaning of parliamentary politics has been completely lost. The credibility of political parties has been destroyed. The power of the military has increased. Most ordinary Japanese people believe in the authority of the military. Second, military expenditure accounts for 49% of Japan's total national treasury expenditure, and the extraordinary period will continue to be extended. It is said that it will continue to be extended until at least 1938. To what extent will military expenditure be increased? We dare not underestimate the situation. Then the so-called peaceful diplomacy is just a term in diplomatic negotiations. Recalling the eve of the European War, Germany also once touted armed peace. However, its peace was a peace protected by arms. Today's Pacific situation is also similar.

Xiao Shuyu's Opinions on Rural Relief

[Nanjing] Legislative member Xiao Shuyu wrote an article on the poverty and relief of rural areas, which he distributed to all legislative members and domestic scholars. He advocated: (1) The central government should designate a county within Jiangsu Province as an agricultural experimental area, and appoint a special commissioner to be responsible for the experimental work, free from all administrative constraints. (2) The county government should add an agriculture and forestry section or an agriculture and forestry bureau to specialize in land reclamation loans, water conservancy cooperation, agricultural improvement and other matters. (3) Each township in the county should send an agricultural instructor to organize an office, with agricultural loan offices, rent and storage offices for plows and farm tools, agricultural product marketing offices, land reclamation offices, orphanage relief offices, job guidance and seedling storage offices, and agricultural warehouses. The experimental fee should be 300,000 to 400,000 yuan, with 50% for loans, 20% for land reclamation and afforestation, 5% for purchasing plows and farm tools, 10% for improving agricultural production, 10% for water conservancy construction, and 5% for temporary expenses. The outline of the work is investigation, statistics, loans, savings, land reclamation, afforestation, water conservancy, pest control, renting out plows, rural treatment of sick livestock, improving agricultural production, and marketing agricultural products. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Ministry of Finance Plans to Formulate Unified Local Collection Methods

[Nanjing] To streamline local finances and unify local collection agencies, the Ministry of Finance has drafted methods to be sent to the provincial governments, ordering the finance departments to formulate detailed rules. A copy will also be submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. The original report states that the three methods for unifying local collection agencies, as resolved by the Second National Financial Conference, were sent to the provincial governments in June of last year, ordering the provincial finance departments to implement them. Subsequently, fifteen provinces, including Jiangsu, Jiangxi, Guizhou, Yunnan, Sichuan, Henan, Gansu, Shaanxi, Hubei, Qinghai, Hebei, Chahar, and Ningxia, successively reported on the situation. Among them, Shaanxi and Yunnan provinces achieved the best results in actual unified collection. In Shaanxi, all collections are handled by the county governments, while in Yunnan, they are generally handled by the finance bureaus. Jiangxi Province also has a unified scale. The remaining provinces, such as Anhui, Jiangsu, Hebei, Henan, and Hubei, either collect through county governments or finance bureaus, or continue the old practice of contracted merchants. As for Guizhou, Gansu, Chahar, Qinghai, and Ningxia provinces, either the situation is special, or reforms need to be added. The Ministry originally intended to focus on the principle of unification, consider the circumstances, and formulate interim measures as a standard for promotion. Appropriately, the Executive Yuan issued Instruction No. 2562 on January 25th, approving the letter from the Chief of the Military Affairs Commission's Headquarters, sending the outline of the methods for abolishing bureaus and changing to sections in bandit suppression provinces, which was reviewed by the four ministries of internal affairs, finance, real estate, and education, and submitted to the Yuan Affairs Conference, passed as proposed, and sent to the Central Political Committee for record, and submitted to the National Government for record, and handed over to the Legislative Yuan for reference. Article 7 of the original outline stipulates that the reform principle of county financial affairs is in line with the financial conference. The above-mentioned provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, and Henan are all within the bandit suppression area and should comply with the original methods of Shaanxi, which are also the same. The remaining provinces should also formulate implementation rules based on this outline to promote them together. The Ministry originally intended to formulate separate methods, the meaning of which is also the same. In addition to copying the original outline of the methods and the fifth item of the main points of the original letter, it is sent to the provincial governments for reference, ordering the finance departments to refer to the original case, formulate detailed rules, order compliance, and report to the Ministry for record, no later than the start of the budget year of the 24th year, to report all the information. Accordingly, I respectfully request your review and record. (22nd day special telegram)

The Construction and Education Departments have each sent personnel to conduct a survey. (Central News Agency telegram, 22nd)

Anxi Guo Bandits Have Collapsed

[Xiamen] The Ninth Division's Xie Brigade suppressed Guo Zong in Anxi and successively captured seven bandit nests, including Qijingtou, Sanyang, Qinshan, Huaxi, and Xianjingxu. The remaining bandits have collapsed, with a small part hiding in the mountains. 300 weapons have been seized, and Guo's chief of staff has been captured and ordered to collect the remaining troops and search for hidden weapons. It has come to an end. Xie reported to Quanzhou on the 21st. (Special telegram, 22nd)

Japanese Fleet Commander Hyakutake Arrives in Shantou

[Shantou] Hyakutake Genkichi, commander of the Japanese Third Fleet, arrived in Shantou. The mayor and the director of the Public Security Bureau hosted him at the police recreation club and accompanied him to inspect the entire city. He is scheduled to leave Shantou on the 23rd. (Special telegram, 22nd)

Tourism Delegation to the Philippines Arrives in Hong Kong

[Hong Kong] A tourism delegation of 26 people from the Shanghai business community, led by Deputy Head Wang Xiaolai, arrived in Hong Kong at 10:00 AM on the 22nd aboard the Jackson. At 3:00 PM, the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce held a meeting to welcome them. At 7:00 PM, the Bank Association hosted a banquet. The delegation is scheduled to take the original ship to the Philippines on the 23rd. (Central News Agency telegram, 22nd)

[Hong Kong] The Shanghai inspection team to the Philippines arrived in Hong Kong on the morning of the 22nd. At 3:00 PM, they attended a welcome meeting at the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce. International Arms Control Convention

Roosevelt Asks Senate for Unconditional Approval

Aims to Prevent Naval Conflicts in the Persian Gulf

[Washington] President Roosevelt today sent a message to the Senate, requesting unconditional approval of the international arms control treaty. At a time of international naval tension, the President's move is particularly noteworthy. It is said that the President intends to find ways to prevent conflicts between naval powers even in the far-off Persian Gulf. The Senate approved the treaty last year, but with reservations. The President's current request is for unconditional approval of the treaty signed in Switzerland in 1925. The reservation last year was proposed by Senator King, namely that the United States' compliance with the treaty should not be construed as denying Persia's sovereignty over the Persian Gulf. The State Department could not accurately interpret King's intentions, but some quarters feared that Britain would oppose this reservation, as British ships have been patrolling the Persian Gulf for years. The President probably does not want to cause diplomatic conflict between Britain and the United States, especially since the two countries have had disagreements recently on proposals for international control of the arms industry. In the Geneva Arms Committee, the US representative strongly advocated that the control of the arms industry should be handled by a neutral organization formed by various countries. This proposal has many supporters, and even Canada sides with the US against Britain. Therefore, the White House requests unconditional passage of the arms treaty so that the Geneva conference will not be affected. King has not explained in detail what he had in mind when he proposed the reservation, but the government does not want minor matters to hinder the overall situation. Leaders close to the White House in the Senate expect the President's proposal to pass quickly. (National Telegram, 21st)

Austrian Chancellor's First Visit to Paris Since Taking Office

Temporarily Alights Outside City, French Premier Personally Welcomes Guest

Left-Wing Groups Demonstrate at Station, 800 Arrested

Talks to Cover London Agreement Framework

Austria Seeks British and French Aid for Independence Guarantee

[Paris] Austrian Chancellor Dr. Kurt Schuschnigg visited Paris for the first time since taking office. To avoid hostile demonstrations at the station, he got off the train outside Paris and took a car into the city. The military police gathered at the station resembled a fortress. In addition to a large contingent of police, there were patrol teams with rifles and helmets, forming a defensive line outside the station to prevent unauthorized persons from crossing. The authorities are likely taking the assassination of King Alexander of Yugoslavia into consideration, so the precautions are unusually strict. Military police arrested over 800 people outside the station. Anyone who was slow to comply with the order to "move forward" was at risk of being arrested. An hour before the Austrian Chancellor's train arrived, a crowd had gathered outside the station. By then, over 500 people had already been arrested. Most of them were young people who had come to the station to demonstrate against the Austrian Chancellor at the call of the Socialist Communist Party. At 9:11 PM, the Vienna train arrived, and the crowd was greatly disappointed to learn that the Austrian Chancellor was not on the train. When Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Walterberger alighted from the train outside Paris, French Premier Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval personally welcomed them. They then traveled together by car to the hotel. Observers view the Austrian Chancellor's visit as primarily a matter of protocol, just like his recent visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. However, his talks with the French authorities are also of great importance, as they will cover the framework of the major negotiations initiated by the recent Anglo-French agreement, and the Danube Pact is also part of the security guarantees under discussion. (Reuters, 21st)

Franco-Austrian Talks Begin

[Paris] Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger met with Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval this morning, and the meeting ended at 11:10 AM. This visit by the Austrian officials is of a courtesy nature and not an exchange of opinions, but the two sides talked for over an hour, presumably reviewing various issues in brief in order to discuss them in detail later. In the afternoon, they will meet again at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. After parting with Flandin and Laval, the Austrian officials went to the Presidential Palace for a luncheon hosted by President and Mrs. Lebrun. Key figures in diplomatic and political circles, such as Prime Minister Flandin and Foreign Minister Laval, were among those invited. Before the luncheon, the President awarded the Austrian officials the Grand Cross of the Legion of Honor. (Havas, 22nd)

[Paris] The Franco-Austrian talks will inevitably involve the London Agreement, which reiterates the principles of the Rome Agreement regarding the security of the Danube and the non-interference pact, which are of great concern to Austria. The Soviet note stated that 70% of the people of Europe support the London Agreement, and this is indeed the case. (Havas, 21st)

[Paris] This morning, officials from both countries held a meeting and gathered for a banquet at the palace at noon. Their discussions included Austria's political and economic situation and various issues related to the Danube. Reports suggest that the issue of the Habsburg restoration was also discussed. However, the "Wolff Bureau" reported that while the restoration issue is being discussed extensively in Austria, the current government is not actively promoting this movement. However, Schuschnigg advocates not suppressing this issue, as it creates a balance between the National Socialist Party and the monarchists. Therefore, Schuschnigg will express to the French government that he does not support the immediate restoration of the monarchy. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Austrian Prime Minister Visits Britain and France Seeking Equal Status

[Paris] The press is commenting on the visit of Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Berger. "L'Action Française" wrote, "The two Austrian politicians are visiting Paris first, then London, and will discuss various important issues with British and French politicians. One issue that will certainly be discussed is that since the Great War, Austria has always played a passive role on the political stage. Now the Vienna government is eager to break free from this position and intends to seek a path to development while fulfilling the Rome Agreement, so that Austria can be guaranteed by other countries on the one hand, and can also guarantee the countries that guarantee Austria on the other. In other words, Austria wants to join the group of powers with equal rights, and wants to retain absolute freedom in its political relations with its neighbors. Only in this way can Austria be said to be gradually achieving equal status, especially moving towards a policy of multilateral cooperation and opposing bilateral cooperation. The so-called bilateral cooperation is a policy that is contrary to international conventions, which is what the Rome Agreement seeks to correct." (Havas, 22nd)

Resisting Foreign Aggression and Suppressing the Expansion of German Influence

[Paris] Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Austrian Foreign Minister Walter Berger had lengthy talks with the French Prime Minister, and consulted on the peaceful issues of the Anglo-French London Declaration. However, the most important thing is the Anglo-French guarantee of Austria's independence. It is generally said that the purpose of Schuschnigg and Berger's visits to France and Britain is to seek international assistance to suppress the expansion of German influence, and at the same time, other than Italy, only Britain and France can help Austria resist foreign political and territorial aggression. (National Telegram, 22nd)

Laval Meets with Ambassadors from Five Countries

London Suggests Maintaining Contact

Germany's Attitude is a Key Factor

[Paris] Before the Austrian Prime Minister arrived, French Foreign Minister Laval had consulted with the British, Russian, German, Italian, and Polish ambassadors several times. (Reuters, 21st)

[Paris] Foreign Minister Laval met separately today with the Italian, Polish, and German ambassadors to France. The talks were clearly related to the London Agreement. Since yesterday's British cabinet meeting and the Soviet government's note to the British and French governments, there seems to be considerable progress on the point of maintaining mutual contact regarding the various proposals in the Anglo-French London Declaration. During yesterday's London cabinet meeting, the British government confirmed that the London Agreement is a complete plan, and no part of it should be allowed to be separated. It would be inappropriate for Germany's reply to selectively interpret the Air Pact. Later, the note from the Moscow government further indicated that a major European country is willing to provide strong support for this claim (that the various parts of the London Agreement cannot be separated), which is of utmost importance. As for the procedures that countries will follow to conduct negotiations, so that a consensus can be reached on the overall issue in the end, the French side believes that this is a secondary issue. According to reports in British newspapers, after Simon, the British Foreign Secretary, goes to Berlin, he will continue to Moscow via Warsaw, and this news is greatly appreciated here. France has close ties with the Soviet Union and Poland, and is very pleased to see another friendly great power visit the Soviet Union and Poland, thereby increasing the universal nature of the London Agreement. (Havas, 21st)

British Foreign Office Studies Soviet Documents

East European Pact Network Constitutes a Security Factor

Cannot be Effective if Germany and Poland do not Participate

[London] The Soviet government's note on the February 3rd London Declaration is currently being studied in detail by the Foreign Office. According to general observations, the network of pacts among Eastern European countries has become an important factor in security. However, Lithuania and its southeastern neighbors (i.e., Germany and Poland) have not yet signed pacts. If this shortcoming can be remedied, Eastern European security will be even more effective. It is said that people in diplomatic circles are now considering this, which is why rumors are circulating that British officials will stop in Poland on their way from Berlin to Moscow. (Havas, 21st)

Italy Prepared for any Eventuality

On East European Mutual Assistance Pact

Italian View is the Same as Britain's

[Rome] After Germany sent its reply to the Anglo-French proposals, Italian public opinion unanimously stated that the European situation is becoming chaotic and uncertain. The Supreme Defense Council issued a communiqué yesterday, announcing that Italy is prepared for any eventuality, with the intention of reassuring the public. "Foreign Affairs Daily" stated, "Germany's reply indicates that it neither refuses to participate in the fundamental issues, nor does it want to cooperate sincerely. Germany's method is to separate the Air Pact from other issues. However, Britain firmly believes that the East European Mutual Assistance Pact should be freely discussed by the countries concerned, but Britain itself is not bound by it. Italy's view is generally the same as Britain's." The "Genoa Labor News" stated, "It is absolutely impossible to only sign the Air Pact and ignore other issues, because it is not enough to secure the Franco-German border, it is necessary to ensure that other nations no longer fear German aggression." (Havas, 21st)

Changing Situation in East Africa, Italian War Preparations Intensify

Expedition Commander has already Set Off

Japan Indicates it will Definitely not Assist Abyssinia against Italy

Coastal Highway under Construction in the Mediterranean

[Rome] Italy's military precautionary measures for East Africa have not stopped. Italian troops and military supplies are continuously being transported to East Africa to prepare for war with Abyssinia. The 19th Division stationed in Florence will soon be transferred to southern Italian ports to join the 29th Reserve Division currently in Messina, and will be sent to East Africa when necessary. In addition, it is rumored that another large number of troops will set sail from Naples tomorrow. (Havas, 22nd)

Naples: The Italian postal ship "Vulcano", carrying 400 industrial specialists, 700 engineers and sanitation soldiers, and various supplies, is scheduled to set sail from here tomorrow evening for Italian East African colonies (i.e., Eritrea and Italian Somaliland). It will stop briefly at Messina to load more than 1,000 troops stationed there before departing. The commander of the Italian expedition, General Graziani, is also embarking on this ship. He is the youngest general to have earned medals for meritorious service. Previously, the locals in Cyrenaica, Italian Libya, did not submit and often caused disturbances. He was ordered to suppress them, and the entire region was eventually pacified. In the battle of Saisan, the Italian army captured the ancient Fara well in the desert, which was also Graziani's achievement. When he set off today, Crown Prince Vittorio Emanuele III personally saw him off. (Havas, 22nd)

[Rome] Japanese Ambassador to Italy, Shigemitsu, went to Norway today to participate in the Olympic Committee meeting. Before leaving, he told a Reuters reporter that if Italy and Abyssinia go to war, Japan will definitely not assist Abyssinia. Recently, Japan's friendly relations with Abyssinia have intensified, leading to rumors that Japan is preparing to assist Abyssinia against Italy. Shigemitsu's statement is reassuring. At the same time, Italian war preparations continue unabated. (Reuters, 22nd)

[Rome] The coastal highway along the Mediterranean Sea in Italian Tripoli, Africa, is currently under construction and is scheduled to be inaugurated by Prime Minister Mussolini in April 1936. After the road is completed, there will be direct access between Egypt and French Tunisia. (Havas, 21st)

US Giant Bombers Fly Across Continent in Formation

From the East Coast of the Pacific to Washington

Preparations Completed

San Diego: Preparations for the flight of twelve giant US bombers to Washington were completed today. This is the final step from Washington to the Panama Canal Zone. The Martin giant aircraft used this time are the same as those used in the recent formation flight from Washington to Alaska and back to San Diego. This non-stop round-trip flight from San Diego to San Rafael, California, is a test flight, covering a distance of 1,200 miles. Its purpose is to familiarize the pilots with the difficulties of flying to Panama. These giant bombers have a speed of 260 miles per hour, and each can carry 400 gallons of gasoline and thousands of pounds of bombs. Since completing the flight to Alaska, students from the Army Aviation School have been flying them from Rockwell Airfield here to the sea for practice flights. Pilots learn to fly blind, fly far from land, and search for ships at sea using radio and other signals emitted from the flying school. This training was invented by the Army Aviation Department to expand the US coastal defense and extend it deep into the ocean. Although these aircraft have flown thousands of miles over the sea, they have no floatation devices. However, each has two engines, and one engine can keep the aircraft flying in the air. In the future, when flying to Panama, they will communicate with land stations and ships at sea. This flight is intended to test the Army's radio equipment as much as possible. It is said that General McClelland will be in charge of this flight. (National Telegram, 21st)

American One-Eyed Aviator Makes Stratospheric Flight

In the Air 35,000 Feet Above Ground

Departing from Los Angeles, Flying Directly to New York

Los Angeles: Famous one-eyed aviator Wiley Post took off from here today in his plane, the Winnie Mae, intending to reach New York via the stratosphere. This is the same plane he used to fly around the world twice. Post is wearing a specially made "oxygen suit" and plans to fly at an altitude of 35,000 feet, with a planned speed of 350 miles per hour. The purpose of this trip is to test whether the stratosphere can be flown through by commercial aircraft. If successful, it will be a great achievement in the aviation world. (Reuters, 22nd)

Two British Royal Air Force Aircraft Set Off for Singapore

Naples, Italy: Four seaplanes belonging to the British Royal Air Force are flying from England to Singapore. One of them, K3595, crashed on the mountainside near Messina, Italy on the 15th of this month. Another, K3594, has already flown to Malta. Today, the remaining two, K3592 and K3593, also flew from Nisi Island near Naples to Malta to join K3594. (Havas, 22nd)

More Details on the British Airship Accident, Sisters Die for Love in the Air

[London] The two daughters of the American Consul General to Naples, Mr. Bowers, both died in a plane crash. It is widely believed that this is related to the British airship accident near Messina, Italy last week. The younger daughter, Miss Gahan, 20 years old, was engaged to Air Force officer Mr. Forbes, who died in the airship. The elder sister, Elizabeth, 23, was also engaged to another Air Force officer, Mr. Petty, who was also killed in the accident. According to friends of the two daughters, they had been depressed and restless in recent days. They recently hired a plane to travel from England to France for a short trip to relieve their emotions. Unexpectedly, when flying over Essex, they both crashed in a field and died instantly, following their fiancés to the afterlife. Two sealed letters were found in the plane and have been handed over to the London police. The mother of the two daughters said after receiving the bad news that she did not know why her daughters did this. (Reuters, 21st)

Quezon Carries Philippine Constitution Draft to US via Hong Kong

[Hong Kong] Philippine Senate President Quezon is silent about Washington's approval of the Philippine Constitution, but he is confident that it will not encounter difficulties. Quezon and his delegation of Philippine dignitaries, traveling on the President Coolidge to the United States, passed through here today. Quezon said that he sees no reason why the draft constitution should not be approved, as government approval of the case does not conflict with precedent. If a responsible government can be established, the Philippines will definitely enjoy its benefits. He hopes that the new constitution can take effect before the end of this year. Philippine Governor Murphy, who is currently in the United States meeting with President Roosevelt, recently stated here that he considers the Philippine Constitution drafted by the special conference to be a model code. (National Telegram, 22nd)

International Business Telegram

February 22nd Reuters Exclusive Business Report

US Markets All Closed

Today (Friday) is the birthday of George Washington, the first President of the United States, and the entire country is celebrating, so all markets are closed.

Gold and Silver

British Gold: London gold prices rose seven and a half pence today to 143 shillings and six and a half pence due to the weakness of the pound.

British Silver: The difference between spot and futures prices for silver in London is large today. The spot price fell .0625 to 25 pence .125, while the futures price remained unchanged at 25 pence .25.

Exchange Rates

London Foreign Exchange: The pound was weak in the London foreign exchange market this morning. Continental Europe sold pounds from morning to noon, causing the US exchange rate to shrink by just over one cent and the French exchange rate to shrink by twenty points.

British-American Exchange: The opening price this morning was $4.87.0625, which was .3125 lower than the closing price of the US-British exchange rate yesterday. It fell .25 at 11:00 AM, and then fell another half-cent at noon to $4.86.3125. At this time, the market situation began to stabilize slightly, and this price was maintained. After 1:00 PM, the number of sellers decreased slightly, and the price rebounded .125 at 2:00 PM to $4.86.4375.

British-French Exchange: The opening price was 72 francs .66, which was three points lower than the previous closing price. It shrank by nine points at 11:00 AM, and then shrank by six points at noon. It fell another four points after 1:00 PM to 73 francs .47. It rebounded three points at 2:00 PM to 73 francs .50.

Cotton and Wheat

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was very calm. At 1:00 PM, the May futures price was 6 pence .82, which was one point lower than the previous closing price.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market rose .125 at 1:00 PM today to 4 shillings and 11 pence .125.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was stable this morning. The near-term price remained unchanged, while the long-term price rose slightly. At noon, the transaction prices for July and September were 6 pence .6875, the same as the previous closing price.

President of Tokyo Yomiuri Newspaper Stabbed and Seriously Wounded

Advocating Constitutionalism, Hated by Right-Wing Groups

Perpetrator Surrenders, Confesses to being Leader of Bushinkai

[Tokyo] At 8:40 AM on February 22nd, Yomiuri Newspaper President Matsutaro Shoriki was about to enter the editorial office at the Yomiuri Newspaper Company in Ginza West 3rd Street when he was suddenly attacked by a suspicious man of about 30 years of age and stabbed with a short knife. He suffered a serious wound to the left neck, 15 cm long and 8 cm deep. Staff in the building immediately sent him to Tsukiji Hayashi Hospital for emergency treatment, but due to excessive bleeding, he is becoming increasingly weak and his life is in danger. The perpetrator surrendered on the spot and was taken to the Marunouchi Police Station. He confessed that his name is Katsusuke Nagasaki and that he belongs to a right-wing ideological group. It is said that the reason for his actions was that the Yomiuri Newspaper recently published an article supporting Dr. Minobe's constitutional theory advocated in the Diet. The company also used a large amount of national funds to invite an American professional baseball team, and President Shoriki was involved in the Tokyo city jail incident, etc. Nagasaki is currently the youth leader of the Bushinkai. The Bushinkai is a right-wing group that advocates royal centralism and has intimidated the Tokyo Nichinichi Newspaper and the Hochi Newspaper. It is a group that the Metropolitan Police Department is guarding against. (Domei News, 22nd)

[Tokyo] Yomiuri Newspaper President Matsutaro Shoriki, who was stabbed at 8:40 AM this morning, is still being treated in the company. He underwent a second blood transfusion at 6:00 PM and is doing better. Shoriki previously served as the chief of the Metropolitan Police Department's General Affairs Division. After retiring, he became the president of Yomiuri. He is also a powerful member of the Banchokai and is close to the protagonist of the rayon case of the Seiyukai, and is a liaison figure between political parties and financial groups. The fascists hate him to the bone. After being released from prison, he wrote about constitutionalism, which led to this assassination attempt. The perpetrator is Katsusuke Nagasaki, the youth leader of the Bushinkai. After the attack, he surrendered himself. (Chinese United Press, 22nd)

Hirota Answers Questions from Yoshizawa, Explains Policy Towards Russia

First Resolve Various Pending Issues

Then Conclude a Non-Aggression Pact

[Tokyo] Foreign Minister Hirota gave the following answers to questions from Kenkichi Yoshizawa (Friends Club) at the secret meeting of the General Budget Committee of the House of Peers yesterday afternoon: (1) Regarding the Russian-Manchurian border defense issue, Japan is originally an island nation and is therefore overly sensitive. If it were in Europe or the United States, border defense would be a matter of course. The Soviet Union is also carrying out defense with this in mind. However, the border defense that Japan is considering is different from what the Soviet Union is considering. However, Japan cannot but give appropriate consideration to the Soviet Union's more than necessary defense. (2) There are two ways to conclude a treaty: (1) to conclude a treaty after resolving various issues between the two countries, and (2) to begin resolving pending issues after concluding a treaty. I believe that it is most appropriate for Japan and Russia to conclude a non-aggression treaty after resolving pending issues. (3) Establishing peace in the Far East is what the government is striving for most. Some people suspect that Japan will unite with Britain or the United States to achieve this goal. I do not advocate establishing a special relationship with any one country. I intend to continue friendly relations with all countries. It is Japan's fundamental policy to establish peace in the Far East by maintaining friendly relations with any country without uniting with one country to oppress another. We will continue to work towards this in the future. (Dentsu News, 22nd)

Soviet Russia Builds Railway Linking Outer Mongolia

Harbin Correspondence: It is said that the Moscow People's Committee for Transportation plans to build a railway between Moscow and Kulun. Negotiations with the Outer Mongolian authorities have been completed, and the first phase of construction has begun, i.e., the laying of the line between Chita, Kulun, and Kulun. The Ussuri Railway tracks are being used to transport cables and other materials, and it is very busy. However, the completion of the line will take several years. However, the construction of the road, in military and economic terms, is a major stimulus for Japan. (Chinese United Press)

Release of Detained Russian Personnel from the Chinese Eastern Railway

[Harbin] Over fifty Soviet Russian staff members of the Chinese Eastern Railway were recently arrested by the authorities of "Manchukuo," accused of engaging in communist conspiracies and plotting to sabotage the railway. They have now been released. Some gentlemen are still being held in detention and are expected to be fully released by the end of this month. (Reuters dispatch, 22nd)

U.S. Economic Mission to Depart for China Next Month

Intending to Stay in Japan for Two Weeks

Expected to Arrive in Shanghai on April 26th

[Washington] The International Trade Association authorities today finalized plans to send an economic survey mission to the Far East. The mission will consist of fifteen leading figures from the international trade industry, who will travel to China for a survey lasting approximately two months. According to an announcement today by the association's chairman, Forbes, and vice-chairman, Thomas, the mission will depart from San Francisco on the President Coolidge on March 22nd, with Forbes and Thomas leading the group. Unofficial sources indicate that the original plan for the mission to visit the Philippines has been abandoned due to the current unstable political situation there. The mission will arrive in Japan at Kobe on April 5th, depart from Kobe on the 19th, and arrive in Shanghai on the 26th. In China, the mission will divide into groups to survey the situation and study all aspects of trade in the interior. It is expected that they will depart from Shanghai to return to the United States around June 18th. (National Telegram, 21st)

Fascist Party Demonstrates in Front of U.S. Embassy in Tokyo

Protesting Anti-Japanese Movement in the United States

[Tokyo] This morning, a Fascist party staged a demonstration in front of the U.S. Embassy, protesting anti-Japanese actions in Arizona, USA. Six people were arrested at the scene by the police. Today's editorial in the Asahi Shimbun stated that the anti-Japanese trend in Arizona should not be regarded as a local matter. The state legislature has now proposed legislation to exclude Japanese people. For the sake of U.S.-Japan friendship, the U.S. authorities must abolish this barbaric bill. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

U.S. Treasury Secretary Declares No Change in Monetary Policy

Hoover Criticizes New Deal as a Pre-Election Ploy

[Washington] Treasury Secretary Morgenthau stated today at a press conference that the government is currently satisfied with its monetary policy and does not wish to make any changes. The government will continue to work along its current path. Although former President Hoover advocates restoring the gold standard and stabilizing the dollar at its current value, the government does not intend to alter its course. Hoover's remarks did not generate much interest today, so the markets remain unexciting. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

[Washington] Former President Hoover's statement yesterday in Tucson on restoring the gold standard was only a fleeting moment. Washington has returned to calm today. Most quarters consider Hoover's statement to be the opening salvo of his 1936 presidential campaign. Republican leaders have remained silent on the matter, but it is said that the conservative elements of the party also regard Hoover as their leader. Some political observers believe that Hoover's statement aims to make restoring the gold standard the platform of the Republican Party's 1936 presidential campaign, while others believe that Hoover merely intends to offer his personal judgment to the country. The New Deal faction immediately launched a counter-reaction. Senator Lenna LaRoux attacked Hoover in the Senate, criticizing Hoover for hastily criticizing his resumption of the presidency and stating that Hoover's policies were those that led to the collapse of his government. (National Telegram, 21st)

U.S. Silver Purchase Statistics

[Washington] According to figures released today by the Department of Commerce, U.S. silver imports for the week ending February 15th were lower than before. The value of silver imported this time totaled $5,051,683, compared to $7,005,000 the previous week. The United Kingdom remains the main supplier and continues to be the purchasing market for the United States. The amount purchased from the UK this time was $3,269,440, compared to $6,176,000 the previous week. Mexico still occupies a prominent position in the report. The value of silver exported this time was $1,338,745, compared to only $209,000 the week before February 8th. Hong Kong also imported silver into the United States, supplying a total of $198,115. In the past three weeks, Hong Kong has supplied a total of $807,155. The Federal Reserve Board today released a report stating that the amount of silver certificates in circulation in the United States in 1934 increased by $189,000,000. As of December 31st of last year, there were approximately $580,000,000 in silver certificates in circulation in the market. However, the actual increase in silver dollars in circulation last year was only $2,000,000. By the end of last year, there were a total of 31,000,000 silver dollars. The value of subsidiary coins in circulation at the end of last year totaled $287,000,000, an increase of $20,000,000 compared to the previous year. (National Telegram, 21st)

[New York] A large batch of silver, totaling about 90 tons, arrived here today from London, almost all of which was purchased by the U.S. Treasury Department. It is found that within one week ending February 15, the total value of silver imported into the United States was US$5,052,000, most of which came from England, with a total value of US$3,269,000. The rest came from Mexico, worth US$1,339,000; from Honduras, worth US$58,000; from Peru, worth US$131,000; and from Canada, worth US$17,000. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

Roosevelt Encourages People to Eat Fish

Glamorous Women's Parade as a Promotional Campaign

[Washington] President Roosevelt has recently appointed former physical education professor McFadden to conduct a nationwide promotional campaign to encourage people to eat more fish and increase fish consumption. McFadden will serve as a member of the Department of Commerce's advisory committee, leading a large group of beautiful women to travel around the country, so that people in the interior can witness the beauty and realize the practical benefits of eating fish, which are beneficial to both health and beautification. According to the Department of Commerce, Americans tend to prefer meat. Although eating fish can supplement food, it cannot replace meat. Americans currently eat an average of 15 pounds of fish per person per year, while Japanese people eat 55 pounds and Swedes eat as much as 50 pounds. (Havas dispatch, 21st)

Vegetarian Diet in the Countryside Leads to Longevity

Centenarians Abound in Bulgaria

[Vienna] Bulgaria is a country of long-lived people. The country has a population of only six million, but according to official surveys, there are 162 people over the age of one hundred. This percentage of long-lived people is unique in the world. In addition, there are probably three or four hundred people who claim to be one hundred years old but have not actually confirmed their age. The reasons for such longevity are currently being studied by doctors and scientists and are quite interesting. First, all the people in Bulgaria who are over one hundred years old are farmers. None of them live in cities, and most of them are shepherds in the mountains. From this, it can be seen that the difficult and arduous life in the mountains is enough to improve people's health. Secondly, these centenarians are not tall or strong. At the same time, they marry very early, mostly between the ages of twenty and twenty-five. Almost none of them marry after the age of thirty-five. They also have many children, averaging 7.4. Vegetarianism seems to be related to longevity. Among these 162 people, 95 percent never eat meat, 3 percent occasionally taste meat, and only 2 percent eat meat and vegetables together. About 80 percent have the habit of drinking alcohol, while only 20 percent do not drink alcohol, so alcohol does not have a major impact on human health. As for tobacco, most do not smoke. Among these 161 people, 85 are women and 77 are men. Among them, there is a shepherd who is currently 121 years old and is still as strong as ever. (National Telegram, 22nd)

The Secret of the Night-Flying Man Is Uncovered

Merchant Wanted to Sell an Island for a Good Price

Norwegian Military Police Investigation Cost a Lot

Norwegian City The secret of the night-flying man, which was widely reported in the newspapers last year, has now been uncovered. Last year, the Norwegian newspapers had numerous reports about this mysterious aviator, saying that he was flying along the northern coast of Norway at night, but it was difficult to find his whereabouts. However, it has now been discovered that the rumor was actually fabricated by a merchant. Several years ago, the merchant obtained ownership of an island called "Jan Mayen." The island is located in the sea north of Norway. The merchant then thought of selling the island to the Norwegian government and fantasized about creating all kinds of sensational news to attract the attention of the Norwegian government authorities, so they would know that the island had value as an aviation base. It is said that the merchant even contacted the Soviet Russian and Japanese authorities to threaten the Norwegian government, so they would know that other governments had covetous intentions. After the merchant's secret was discovered, the Norwegian government has begun an investigation and may file a lawsuit against the merchant, because after the news of the night-flying man spread, the Norwegian army, navy, and police spent a lot of money on investigating and patrolling the matter. (National Telegram, 21st)

British Shipping Subsidy Bill Passed Third Reading in the Upper House

[London] The shipping subsidy bill of £2 million passed its third reading in the House of Lords today. It will become law after the King approves it. The main point of this bill is to use the subsidy to enable British ships without fixed routes to compete with subsidized foreign ships as much as possible, so that foreign shipping can be forced to cooperate with British merchants to seek ways to adjust the supply and demand of world shipping. (Reuters dispatch, 21st)

Completion Ceremony of the Shanghai Battle Memorial Tower for the 88th Division

[Hangzhou] The memorial tower for the fallen soldiers of the 88th Division in the Shanghai Battle, located on the shore of West Lake, held a solemn completion ceremony at 9:00 AM on the 22nd amidst dark clouds. A ceremony platform was set up in front of the tower, with the horizontal inscription "The Spirit Moves Rivers and Mountains." On both sides were military music platforms. Recalling the past events, he felt even more grief. Northwestern Inspection Record

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya of this Newspaper

An Overview of the Transformations in Xinjiang in Recent Years (1)

Xinjiang is isolated and located in a remote region, nestled between the two major powers of Britain and the Soviet Union. Its borders directly abut foreign countries, stretching over four thousand hundreds of miles. Since 1931 (Western calendar), with the successful construction of the Turkestan-Siberia Railway by the Soviet Union, connecting to the Siberian Railway, the northwestern part of Xinjiang, namely the heartland of the new province, has become increasingly entrapped in a situation where others are near while we are far, others are at ease while we are burdened. Xinjiang's diplomacy has always been arduous, and now, with the rapid evolution of the international situation, it is even more difficult, needless to say. Looking back at the internal residents, the ethnic groups are extremely complex. In the southern part of the Tianshan Mountains, they are called "Chantou" and "Brut," which constitute the majority. In the northern part of the Tianshan Mountains, they are called Mongol, Kazakh, and Hui (also known as Gan Hui or Han Hui; the Chantou are called Dungan), which constitute the majority. As for the Manchus, Solons, Sibos, Andijanis, Tunguses (a mixed race of Han Chinese and Turks), and naturalized Russians, etc., scattered in the north and south of Xinjiang, their numbers are also considerable. Not to mention the resident foreigners from the Soviet Union, Britain, France, Italy, Germany, the United States, Portugal, the Netherlands, India, Turkey, etc. The Han Chinese residing among them are but a small fraction. In terms of residents, it is nothing less than a world exhibition of human races.

Due to geographical relations, Xinjiang is vulnerable to the direct influence of international politics, economy, and other factors. Internally, due to the complexity of residents and the diversity of beliefs, governance is inherently more difficult. In addition, culture is backward, customs are backward and closed, and indigenous people especially like to adhere to the old ways. Since the establishment of schools in the early Republic, government offices have mostly regarded them as mere formalities, and the people have even considered their children's entry into schools as corvée labor, often closing their doors tightly and refusing to comply. As a result, after more than twenty years of educational founding, it still only has a rudimentary form, with no progress. In terms of national character, it is like any other nation in the world, with both strengths and weaknesses. The Kazakhs are naturally strong and belligerent. The Chantou people are docile and hardworking, and usually amiable like family members. However, their cultural knowledge is at a lower level, and they are fond of excitement and easily swayed by "chieftains." One call brings thousands of responses, making it easy to cause incidents. The Qianlong era, the Guangxu era, and the recent years of popular revolts in various counties are evidence of this. Since the residents of Xinjiang are of mixed races, and their nature is ignorant and fond of excitement, if governance is flawed, it will cause major changes, often leading to disasters that last for several years. The history of previous generations can be seen from the historical records. Since diplomatic problems will become increasingly difficult, local authorities should be cautious in their actions, and the central government must quickly plan effective strategies for consolidating border defenses and stabilizing the hinterland, providing timely instructions. As the saying goes, it is not too late to mend the fold after the sheep is lost. This is precisely the time to do so. In order to clarify the facts of the past for future measures to learn from, I will review the past events and write this article.

Yang Zengxin, the former chairman of Xinjiang, had been in office in Xinjiang for many years and knew the local situation very well. When he governed Xinjiang, the policies he implemented were tailored to the local conditions, bordering on fooling the people, resulting in mixed praise and criticism. During Yang's seventeen years in Xinjiang, the area was pacified, the people lived in peace, residents could sleep peacefully, and travelers had no worries on the road. During the Republic of China years five and six, the spirit of his politics was especially commendable. It is a pity that he devoted himself to metaphysics in his later years, seeming to be deluded by the doctrine of "inaction," and failed to take advantage of the opportunity to plan fundamental strategies for consolidating border defenses and raising the culture of the frontier, which was a great mistake. However, Yang still had a self-awareness, once saying, "I only know to obey the central government and do not ask who is in power." During the Beijing government era, he supported it. In the autumn of 1928, when the Northern Expeditionary Army settled in Tianjin, he also telegraphed his support for the National Government and reorganized the provincial government, raising the flag with the blue sky, white sun, and red earth. This shows that he knew that the province could not survive independently from the central government. Yang had considered this carefully. Yang, over sixty years old, once had the intention to retire, but was hesitant due to the province's finances and the selection of a proxy. Instead, he pledged himself with the eight characters "Loyal to Xinjiang, End in Xinjiang." Not long after, he was unfortunately assassinated by his subordinates Fan Yaonan and Zhang Chunxi, who wanted to innovate, while attending the graduation ceremony of the political and legal school. At that time, Jin Shuren, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, quelled the chaos and succeeded as chairman, concurrently serving as the border defense supervisor of Xinjiang. His initial measures also followed the old rules, but Jin's political skills were far inferior to Yang's. During his four or five years in office, he made no achievements and ultimately stepped down in disgrace in 1933 in the so-called "April 12 Incident." According to the formation of this coup, the establishment of a county in Hami and the rebellion of the mountain Chantou were a powerful fuse, but in terms of the establishment of the county, it does not seem to be entirely unjustified. During the Qing Dynasty, the Hami Chantou were governed by a Jasak prince. The prince was enfeoffed because "Bo Ke Erbeidolela" of Hami had contributed to capturing the Jungars during the Qianlong era. The Qing court enfeoffed him as a first-class Jasak prince. In the early Tongzhi period, when the prince "Bo Xier" was martyred, the Qing court also conferred the title of hereditary prince and allowed him to eat his own fiefdoms and have a national salary. According to the Xinjiang Chronicles, in the Ming Dynasty, his subordinates were originally divided into two kings, Loyal and Obedient, within and outside the mountains. Although they later belonged to one king, the thoughts and behaviors of the people within and outside the mountains were fundamentally different. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the hereditary system was still continued. Yuan Shikai, in his plot to become emperor, added the title of "Shamu Husote" twin prince, namely the so-called Sha prince. The Sha prince was autocratic and greedy, and the corvée and taxes were heavy. He strictly controlled the wasteland within Hami, not only not allowing Han Chinese to reclaim it, but also not allowing Chantou people to cultivate it. Whenever he saw fertile land or strong cattle and sheep, he would seize them. There were often additional charges for checking the land and collecting rent every year. Many sheep were not allowed to be less after the autumn check. If they were less, they would be heavily fined as usual. The herders were exploited and had fewer sheep. In order to cleverly avoid heavy fines, they had to turn to each other and gather together to make up the number. His harsh collection and harming of the people was like this. Therefore, the awakened elements of his subordinates had long harbored the intention to rebel. In July 1929 and June 1930, they rose up in resistance twice, but were quelled by the concession of the prince's palace. In July of that year, the Chantou people spontaneously petitioned to change to return to the central government, eager to break away from the bondage of the Hui prince and pay taxes in the same way as the Han Chinese, so as to avoid the prince's demands. At that time, when the Sha prince passed away, the young prince Nie Zier succeeded to the throne, who was addicted to alcohol and smoking, which violated the religious regulations and did not win the hearts of the people. Jin regarded Hami as the gateway to the new province, where there was wasteland everywhere, and the refugees from Gansu who fled to Xinjiang were constantly streaming in. For the sake of reclaiming wasteland and populating the border, he accepted the request of the Chantou people and sent officials to investigate the land and household registration, dividing Hami into the three counties of Yi Wu, Yi He, and Hami in October. The young prince Nie Zier then went to the province himself, requesting more support for the Gongeer land and winter and summer grazing grounds. This is the origin of the change of governance in Hami and Nie Zier's entry into the province. Yao Le Bo Shi, who was serving as the commander of the Five Prefectures "Bo Ke" and the commander of the Chantou soldiers' camp, had been widely rumored in Guannei that he had accompanied Nie Zier to the province to promote the change of governance, but this was not the case. (To be continued)

Luan County Militia Conflict Subsided

Liu Zuo Zhou Incorporates the Militia

Gao Cong Shan Gathers a Crowd to Resist

Tianjin Correspondence The first general team of the Luan County garrison war zone security team clashed with the third district militia of Gao Congshan and Yin Zhisan in the county. As of the 19th, after Luan County chief Chen Cengshi, Lanyu administrative commissioner's office secretary Lin Zhiming, and local gentry tried their best to mediate, the dispute has subsided. The more than 1,000 security team members under Liu Zuozhou have been transferred back to the county seat, most of whom are still in the Bencheng area, taking a surveillance attitude towards the retreating militia. The militia retreated to the third district due to heavy casualties in the continuous fierce battles. The head of the regiment, Gao Congshan, and the deputy head of the regiment, Yin Zhisan, were captured by the security team, along with more than 100 village chiefs and deputies in the third district, all of whom were escorted into the city. The incident has come to an end. As for how to deal with the aftermath, the Ji Province government and county branch have issued orders, instructing the Lanyu administrative commissioner Tao Shangming and Luan County chief to handle it properly. Tao Shangming arrived in Tianjin by night train from Ping on the 19th, visited Yu Xuezhong early on the 20th, asked for instructions, and then took a car back to Tangshan to plan and proceed.

The cause of this conflict was that since last winter, Liu Zuozhou wanted to govern the entire territory of the Luan County militia without a provincial order, and reorganized the regiments into nine districts, appointing his cronies to serve as captains of each team, forcing local people to bear the military expenses and pay them on a monthly basis, which made the local people uneasy. The head of the third district militia, Gao Congsan, and the deputy head of the regiment, Yin Zhisan, secretly expanded their strength to resist. Recently, they had more than 1,000 people. On the 15th of this month, they broke through the siege and attacked the militia of Wang Ying, Le Ying, Ma Tun, and other five villages in the fourth district, confiscating their weapons. The team, which was reorganized by Liu Zuozhou, had more than 20 captains, all of whom were captured and transported to the third district in seven large carts. Passing through Bencheng, there were also hundreds of militia reorganized by Liu Zuozhou stationed there. Gao Yin also led the crowd to attack. They clashed with the local militia outside the north gate. Liu Zuozhou received the news and immediately sent a cavalry squadron to aid. A fierce battle broke out on the 16th. The militia had a larger number of people. After three hours of fierce battle, Liu's troops could not resist and dozens of them were killed. They then retreated. On the 17th, Liu Zuozhou personally led more than 1,000 troops to the scene of the conflict, supervising his troops to attack. That night, there was another fierce battle, with casualties on both sides. On the evening of the 18th, the conflict broke out again. The security team suppressed the militia with the power of artillery fire, causing the militia to suffer 60 or 70 deaths. The war stopped in the early morning of the 19th. Chen Cengjie, the magistrate of Luan County, Lin Zhiming, secretary of the Lanyu Administrative Inspectorate, and Councilor Zhu, and other gentry from Luan County went to Bencheng, trying their best to mediate. The militia handed over the weapons confiscated from the security team and the militia of Wang Ying and other five villages, and disbanded each team. Bencheng was guarded by the security team. Liu Zuozhou began to have no objection, so he led a unit back to the county. On the evening of the 19th, Chen, the magistrate of Luan County, hosted a banquet in the county government to entertain the gentry in the third district and the gentlemen who mediated the matter, inviting Liu Zuo, Lin Zhiming, and others to celebrate and release their suspicions. The dozen or so people, including Gao Congshan, Yin Zhisan, and the village chiefs and deputies who were arrested by the security team, were promised by Liu Zuozhou to be sent to the Lanyu Commissioner's Office for transfer to the court for handling. A storm was considered to have subsided. (20th)

Taiwan's Rice Production Increases Six Hundred Times

Japanese Cultivated Land is Converted to Industrial Products

Encouraging Rice Cultivation in Taiwan to Provide Relief

Xiamen Correspondence Taiwan has vigorously encouraged agricultural production by the Japanese in recent years, especially paying attention to rice and sugar. Rice is for the consumption of Japan, because the population of Japan is increasing day by day, and the cultivated land in the country is mostly converted to industrial agricultural products. Therefore, rice cultivation is particularly encouraged in Taiwan to make up for the lack of rice food in the country. Because Taiwan is located in the subtropics, the climate is mild, and the rainfall is suitable, two seasons of rice can be planted every year, the so-called early rice and late rice, which the Japanese call the first and second phases. According to the latest announcement by the Colonial Industry Bureau of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, the actual income of the first phase of rice last year (Showa 9) was 4,511,046 stones, and the actual income of the second phase was 4,577,480 stones. The total harvest for the rest of the year was 9,088,816 stones, which is the highest record since Taiwan existed. Compared with the actual income of 8,361,839 stones in the previous year, it increased by 727,047 stones. It was also found that the harvest of Penglai rice in the tenth year of the Taisho era (the tenth year of the Republic of China) was only 7,296 stones. Compared with the actual income of 4,286,280 stones last year, the actual increase in production was 600 times. Penglai rice is a kind of rice, that is, what the Japanese eat. (February 21)

Ongoing Road and Water Conservancy Projects in Fujian Province

—Zhangxia Railway also planned for construction—

Tongzhou Dispatch: After the recovery of the bandit areas in northwestern Fujian Province, road construction has been slow due to the lack of a unified command. The Department of Construction, recognizing this, has established the Zhanglongting Area Highway Engineering Office in Longyan to oversee road construction in northwestern Fujian. The entire line is divided into four sections, with construction undertaken by military engineering units. The first section, from Longyan to Liancheng, is built by the 83rd Division's suppression force; the second section, from Longyan to Yongding, is built by the 11th Division's Li Mo'an unit; the third section, from Liancheng to Yong'an, is undertaken by the 45th Division's Dai Minquan; and the fourth section, from Liancheng to Changting, is undertaken by the 36th Division's Song Xilian unit. The area highway office dispatches engineers to guide each section. Furthermore, banditry frequently occurs on the highways in northern and southern Fujian, with repeated incidents of vehicle robberies, which greatly impede traffic. The Department of Construction has received approval from the provincial government to organize six highway patrol teams, each with 200 members. Three teams are stationed on the roads in southern Fujian, and three teams are stationed on the roads in northern Fujian, specifically to protect vehicles. The monthly cost is 20,000 yuan, with the provincial government and the Ministry of Military Affairs each responsible for half. Meanwhile, the Provincial Highway General Engineering Office has established an engineering team, divided into bridge and culvert stone masonry groups, each with 200 people, specifically to repair and improve the roads in the rest of the province. The monthly cost is 12,000 yuan. Both teams are expected to be established within approximately three months. The Zhangxia Railway was suspended in 1932 due to mismanagement, and the Department of Construction sent personnel to manage it. Although overseas Chinese merchants from Southeast Asia proposed raising funds for construction, it did not materialize due to political changes. Now, the Department of Construction is planning to rebuild it, proposing to divide the entire line into two sections. The first section, from Xiamen to Zhangzhou, will be repaired and reopened first. The second section, from Zhangzhou to Changting, will be constructed depending on the circumstances. The provincial government has consulted the Ministry of Railways to send personnel to Fujian to jointly assess the remaining assets of the Zhangxia Railway to begin preparations.

In addition, regarding water conservancy, the provincial government has expanded the Committee for Dredging the Min River into the Provincial Water Conservancy General Engineering Office, under the jurisdiction of the Department of Construction, and appointed Yang Tingyu as its director. The plan is to first build a wharf at Majiang Luoxing Pagoda to accommodate seagoing vessels, with a budget of 200,000 yuan, which has been requested from the Central Bank. Furthermore, the Min River waterway, from Fuzhou to Yanping, is divided into three branches: one to Shunchang, one to Shaxian, and one to Jian'ou. The number of steamboats operating on the river is increasing daily, and competition is becoming increasingly fierce, causing extreme disorder in navigation. A Min River Transportation Office has been established to regulate all steamboats on the Min River. The office will determine the schedules, cabin assignments, and fares of all ships, and no arbitrary changes are allowed. The Department of Construction has appointed Guo Zeshou, the former president of the Bank of China in Fuzhou, as manager, and the office will open within days. Chen Ticheng, the head of the Department of Construction, recently traveled to Shanghai and then to Nanjing on the Taishun steamboat to negotiate with the National Economic Commission for the allocation of road construction funds, with the Ministry of Military Affairs for the organization of highway patrol teams, with the Ministry of Railways to discuss the construction of the Zhangxia Railway, and with the Ministry of Communications to report on the establishment of the Min River Transportation Office. He is expected to return to Fujian in about three weeks. (February 20)

Lunan Taiwei Road Yi River Bridge Completed

1,300 meters long

Construction cost of 180,000 yuan

Jinan Dispatch: The Taiwei Motor Road, from Yixian Taierzhuang to Weixian, is the main line in southern Shandong and has the longest route. After the earthwork was completed, operations began, and the bridges and culverts were continuously constructed. A Bridge Engineering Office was established to divide the entire road into six major sections to supervise construction. The total construction cost is 800,000 yuan. Smaller culvert and bridge projects in each section have been completed in succession. However, the Yi River Bridge outside the east gate of Linyi in the second section is a large project, 1,300 meters long, and is a reinforced concrete overflow bridge. It is the largest bridge on the motor roads in the province. The construction cost is estimated at 180,000 yuan. The project was supervised by Liu Junzhe, the engineer of the road section, and Chen Yuncong and Men Xien, the engineers of the sub-sections. Construction began in October 1933 and lasted for one year and four months. It is now fully completed. After receiving the report, the Department of Construction dispatched Hu Xueji, a technician from the civil engineering group, to the site for acceptance inspection.

Wuxi

Gentry from Liyang Come to Wuxi to Beg for Spring Relief

Since Liyang suffered a drought last year, misery is everywhere, and starvation is rampant. Yesterday, gentry from the county, Di Jianren, Di Xizhi, Shi Cantang, etc., came to Wuxi to solicit spring relief. They stayed at the New World Hotel and made initial contact with local philanthropists Tang Wenzhi, Tang Baoqian, Cai Jian-san, etc. According to Di, only about 10,000 mu of Liyang's million mu of farmland yielded a harvest. Large numbers of people have gone out to seek a living. Those who have not gone out cannot get enough to eat at home. Those who can fill their stomachs with bran and greens are considered to be doing well. Those below that only eat tree bark and grass roots. Therefore, the number of people starving to death each month is very large, and many cattle have also starved to death. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented. They deeply hope for assistance from all sectors of society.

Qing-Dynasty Gift Jade Ruyi Stolen

Xue Fengjie, a deceased local gentry who once served as a magistrate during the late Qing Dynasty, whose mother was an adopted daughter of Empress Dowager Cixi, and who repeatedly entered the palace, had many treasures bestowed upon him by the emperor. His residence on Xueqian Street in the city was burgled the night before last, and a jade ruyi bestowed by the emperor, a liver-colored porcelain vase, and many clothes were stolen, resulting in significant losses. A report has been filed for investigation. Also, the home of Chen Zhanru, a local gentry in Xiaolou Lane in the city, was burgled last night, and clothes, antiques, utensils, and other items worth more than one hundred yuan were stolen. Thieves are rampant in the city, and residents cannot sleep peacefully at night.

Girl Burned to Death in Anjia Village Fire

In Anjia Village, located about three miles west of Zhangjing Bridge in the Seventh District, there are more than 20 households. The home of An Wenkui (An serves at the Shanghai Shanghai Bank) in the village suddenly caught fire around 11 o'clock the night before last. Because it was late at night, no one knew about it, which led to it being uncontrollable. Only one fire-fighting water dragon arrived to put out the fire, resulting in the burning of more than 20 houses of five families, including An Hengbin and An Aduan, dozens of dan of white rice, and one large pig. Wenkui's eldest daughter, named Li Shang, who was only nine years old, did not escape and was tragically burned to death. The loss was quite significant.

Shen Jianchang Inspects Huangtian Port

The construction of the Huangtian Port Southern Canal is imminent. Chen Dingzhi, director of the Zhenwu Canal Work Relief Office, came to Cheng the day before yesterday under the order of Shen, the head of the Construction Department, to guide all engineering matters. The dam site is determined to be in front of the new customs at the port. The entire project is divided into two parts. The first section runs from the port to Nanzha. If it is completed, the second section will be carried out in the second half of the year, running from Nanzha to Sihe Lock. Regarding funding issues, Wu Shuying, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, went to Wuxi again on the 21st to shake hands with various banks to borrow money. Shen Baixian, head of the Construction Department, inspected the Zhenwu Canal work relief. In the afternoon, he took the provincial government's No. 6 car, first arriving in Wujin, and arrived in Cheng at 3 o'clock. He first went to Huangtiankou to inspect the dam site, which he considered satisfactory. He then went to the county government to talk with County Chief Yan and He Peixuan and other members of the engineering office. He said that the spring tide was approaching and that the dredging project must be carried out quickly so that it could be completed within the prescribed time, so that the budget would not be wasted. At about 4 o'clock, Director Shen took the original car to Wuxi to participate in the Lingye Lecture and then went to the province.

Changzhou

Gambling Arrest at Fengshu Bridge Causes Riot

Huang Yongcheng, a patrol officer from the 7th Police Station of Wuyi Yuncun Town, received a report on the 21st that there was gambling activity in Fengshu Bridge. At about 1 p.m., he sent patrol chief Ling Chengzhai to lead eight policemen to arrest the gamblers. Many gamblers and gambling equipment such as pai gow and mahjong were seized on the spot. Just as they were about to be taken away, Jiang Yuquan, the ringleader, stepped forward, ordered an assault, and beat the gong to gather a crowd, claiming to capture bandits. Hundreds of people gathered to surround and beat the police, stripping them of their uniforms and seizing their firearms. As a result, Jiang Yuquan ordered the patrol chief and three policemen to be tied up and sent to the Mingfeng patrol team, falsely claiming that they had captured bandits. The team, considering the case to be serious, handed Jiang Yuquan and the patrol chief over to the city Public Security Bureau for interrogation. However, the whereabouts of five policemen are still unknown. Two wooden-cased guns and one rifle are missing. The patrol chief and others were seriously injured. Director Xu Baoguang is investigating the matter.

Bandits Take Revenge and Mistakenly Kill Village Head

Hangzhou

Garrison Headquarters Officially Abolished

Hangzhou is the capital of Zhejiang Province, and the local security is important. In September 1933, the Provincial Capital Martial Law Headquarters was ordered to be abolished and replaced by the Hangzhou Garrison Headquarters to eliminate reactionaries, punish bandits, eliminate drugs, and maintain public order. After two years, Yu (Jishi), the commander, believed that the remnants of bandits in southeastern Jiangxi and southern Anhui had been eliminated, and local security was no longer a concern. The Hangzhou Garrison Headquarters was deemed unnecessary, and the Military Affairs Commission approved its official abolition, to be completed by the end of this month. Unfinished matters will be transferred to the Security Office for handling.

Gu Guangxin, a businessman in Dingzha Town, suffered significant losses due to illness last year, accumulating heavy debts. Her nerves suddenly broke down, and she used a kitchen knife to cut her throat and died. All who heard of it were saddened.

Loan Contraction Avoids Repeating Mistakes

The banking and currency industries, after the 1934 general disaster relief, have contracted all types of loans, especially credit loans, and the industrial and commercial sectors have been quite vocal against them, but according to reporters from the Xin Sheng News Agency, this is actually a misunderstanding, because although the banking and currency industries were fortunate to make a profit last year, they inevitably suffered bad debts. For example, banks such as Tongyi Jiande and huahua banks such as Baodayudechang were unable to turnover and closed down. The market this year is still depressed, especially more so than last year. Now, for their own sake, they have contracted all types of loans to avoid repeating their mistakes. This is inevitable.

Three Reasons for Market Downturn

The reasons for the market downturn are roughly: (1) affected by the overall global economic recession; (2) the decline of China's rural areas and lack of purchasing power; (3) since the US government nationalized silver, a large amount of silver flowed out of China. Although the government has set up a foreign exchange stabilization committee, increased the silver export tax and balance tax, encouraged foreign silver imports in the future, and tried to revive the countryside and support the development of industry and commerce, it is difficult to recover in a short time due to the excessive damage.
