Grains Association Announces to the Industry to Temporarily Postpone Continuing to Order Foreign Rice

The Existing Foreign Rice Is Sufficient for Six Months of Need

Further Orders Will Lead to a Surplus

According to Dagong News Agency, the Municipal Grains and Oilcake Industry Association, in view of the alarming number of foreign rice orders in the city in the past, issued a notice to the industry on the 28th of last month to pay attention. Now, the association believes that foreign rice is being shipped to Shanghai one after another. If the orders are not stopped, there will be a surplus. Yesterday, it re-announced to the industry to temporarily postpone ordering, the original text said: It is found that the association previously reported to the foreign companies that the amount of foreign rice ordered has reached more than 6.3 million bags. Whether it is necessary to continue to order is considered to require attention, and has been announced for everyone to know and has been submitted to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau for verification. Now, according to the sales of foreign rice, on average, 20,000 bags are sold to other provinces every day, and 5,000 bags are sold locally, for a total of six months until mid-August of the Gregorian calendar. The total sales will be about 4.5 million bags. Currently, it is found that of the 6.3 million bags of foreign rice ordered, in addition to the 1.8 million bags sold earlier, there are about 4 million bags that are still being shipped or have been ordered but not yet shipped. Together with the 500,000 bags currently in stock, the total is 4.5 million bags, which is roughly equivalent to the estimated sales. If the order can be temporarily postponed, the risk of excessive supply and demand can be avoided. It is hereby announced that all industry members should temporarily postpone re-ordering foreign rice under the current circumstances. This is essential. It is hereby notified.

實業部規定國貨展覽品免税辦法

Ministry of Industry Stipulates Tax Exemption Measures for Domestic Product Exhibits

Certificate Should Be Obtained from the Ministry

In order to promote domestic products, the Ministry of Industry has re-stipulated the tax exemption and fee reduction measures for domestic product exhibits. It was reported to the Shanghai Municipal Government yesterday. According to the case, the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in order to promote domestic products, urged provinces and cities to hold exhibitions and display halls, and go to overseas competitions to encourage production. It had formulated five-link tax exemption certificates and railway and steamer fee reduction orders, along with filling-in methods, which were submitted for approval and filed, and were separately approved by the Ministries of Finance, Railways, and Communications for printing. When holding exhibitions in various places and soliciting products or soliciting exhibits, the competent authorities in each place would submit the matter for record and issue them for use. Now, the certificates and shipping orders are about to be used up, and the relevant departments have been consulted to reprint them. All remaining certificates and shipping orders printed by the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce should be abolished immediately. In addition, Article 2 of the previously ordered filling-in method has also been revised due to the opinions of the Ministries of Finance and Railways. In addition to separate consultations, five copies of the revised filling-in method are enclosed for your reference, and it is hoped that you will instruct your subordinates to comply. Attached is the filling-in method for tax exemption certificates and fee reduction orders. Article 1: All those who comply with the General Rules for Holding Goods Exhibitions Nationwide promulgated by the National Government and the Organizational Outline of the National Goods Exhibition Halls of Provinces and Cities approved by the Ministry of Industry, or who are preparing to go to overseas competitions to solicit exhibition and display products, may apply to the Ministry of Industry for tax exemption certificates after approval, and are allowed to be exempt from transit taxes. However, the exemption of export tax and import tax does not apply to this certificate. However, for products sold or transferred to other places at the exhibition site, those with a value of more than 50 yuan must still be taxed in accordance with regulations. In addition, when filling out railway fee reduction orders, national railways should charge 50% of the current ordinary freight rate for exhibits, and 75% for sold products, in accordance with the quantity of exhibits stipulated in the regulations for soliciting products. When filling out steamer fee reduction orders, all routes under the China Merchants Bureau should charge 50% of the current ordinary freight rate. Article 3: Those who receive this tax exemption certificate and fee reduction order should select special personnel to be responsible for safekeeping. For the product solicitation agencies, they must issue the first, second, third, and fourth links based on formal official documents. The issuing specialists must sign and seal the stub link, and prepare a separate list stating the province or city product solicitation agency, how many copies and numbers were received for inspection. Article 4: When the products are shipped, the product solicitation agency should prepare a catalog of the products, listing in detail the names and quantities of the products, attach them to each link, affix a seal on the perforation, indicate the date, and issue the first, second, and third links to the escort to be inspected separately along the way. One side will return the fourth link and the product catalog to the original issuing agency and send it to the Ministry of Industry for record. Article 5: All product exemption certificates and fee reduction orders that have not been filled in after the product solicitation is completed should be returned to the original issuing agency, together with all unissued copies and issued stubs, and sent to the Ministry of Industry for verification to show caution.

浙省推廣植棉計劃

Zhejiang Province Promotes Cotton Planting Plan

Wang Yingbin and Feng Zhaochuan Travel to Nanjing and Shanghai to Negotiate

Wang Yingbin, Secretary of the Zhejiang Provincial Construction Department, recently also served as Director of the Cotton Industry Management Office. The other day, he and Feng Zhaochuan, Deputy Director of the office and Director of the Cotton Field, came to Shanghai from Hangzhou to discuss the purchase of cotton seeds with Chen Guangfu, Zou Bingwen, Deng Fupei, and others from the National Cotton Industry Control Association. According to Mr. Wang, Zhejiang Province's construction undertakings in recent years have been organized on a considerable scale in terms of transportation. Regarding agriculture, it is striving to promote, so it has specially organized an Agricultural Management Committee, which hopes to pay special attention to the cotton industry, so it has also organized a Cotton Industry Management Office. Last year, 20,000 mu of American cotton were trial-planted throughout Zhejiang. This year, it is planned to expand to 150,000 mu. The expansion plan must increase the work by seven times compared to the 20,000 mu work. It is intended that the work will be tense in the future, so it is specially here to consult with the National Cotton Industry Statistics Association. Chen, Zou, Deng, and others from the association all unanimously agreed and tried their best to help, because the results of Zhejiang Province's cotton industry last year were good, and this year it has increased and expanded, and the future results will definitely be predictable. Wang and Feng plan to go to Nanjing by train on the evening of the 24th (Sunday) to request the Ministry of Railways to give special fee reductions when transporting cotton seeds in the future, and immediately go to Zhengzhou to purchase cotton seed work, and also investigate cotton industry experience along the way, preparing for future reference for the expansion and improvement of cotton industry plans. It is believed that the two will make many contributions to the future of Zhejiang Province's cotton industry after returning from Henan this time. According to the investigation, before 1934, the cotton fields for promoting improvement in Zhejiang Province totaled 3,900 mu. After the trial, it was quite effective, so in 1934, it was promoted from 3,900 mu to more than 16,000 mu. The best results were in the coastal American cotton area. Cixi County had an average yield of 189 jin per mu, and even ordinary ones reached more than 150 jin. The general farmers, because they have made considerable profits, have all applied to expand the cotton area. In 1934, the cotton fields for promotion and improvement in Xiaoshan, Hangzhou County, Yuyao, Zhenhai, Cixi, Pinghu, Yinxian, and other counties reached a total of more than 16,730 mu. The total number of harvested seed cotton was 14,890 dan, and the ginned net flower had 4,039 dan. This year, due to disaster relief and the implementation of work relief, it is planned to promote and improve 150,000 mu of cotton fields. In the cotton areas along the Yangtze River, such as Hangzhou County, Xiaoshan, and other counties, 75,000 mu of Million Chinese cotton will be promoted. In the coastal cotton areas, such as Yuyao, Cixi, Zhenhai, and other counties, 65,000 mu of domesticated American cotton will be promoted. In addition, 10,000 mu of Million Chinese cotton and domesticated American cotton will be developed and planted in Shili荒山 and other places in Qu County, inland Zhejiang East, totaling 150,000 mu of promotion. As for the various cotton seeds required for various promotion and improvement plans, they will be selected and purchased by the Cotton Industry Management Office of the Construction Department and distributed to various cotton farmers for collection. Regarding the technical matters of sowing, fertilizing, cultivating, weeding, and harvesting, the office will also specially set up more than 60 instructors at all levels to go to various counties for practical guidance. The harvest results are expected to produce 135,000 dan of cotton in the future, assuming 90 jin per mu. Taking 12 yuan per dan as the price, the total cost is 1.62 million yuan, which is not only higher than that of native cotton, but the proceeds can also be increased by two-tenths. Flower collection, ginning, and transportation, this cotton is all fine velvet cotton, which is suitable for spinning fine yarn of more than 20 counts. It is certain that it will sell well in the future. Moreover, in order to prevent cotton merchants from suppressing prices and retaining seeds (for expanded promotion next year), all matters related to flower collection, ginning, and transportation are handled by the flower collection and ginning factories specially set up by the Cotton Industry Management Office of the Construction Department. Those who do not set up special factories also organize cotton transportation and sales cooperatives to handle it. However, since the flower collection, ginning, and other businesses are complex and require a lot of money, the office also plans to organize a special committee for cotton production management to engage in design and implementation, and work together. It is estimated that 500,000 mu of cotton fields can be promoted next year.

上海國貨公司實施科學管理演講會

Shanghai National Goods Company Holds Lecture on Implementing Scientific Management

Reduced Price Department for Inventory to Be Held Starting Today

Shanghai National Goods Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, after entrusting the China Statistical Design Society to plan scientific management, has drawn up drawings of various departments and determined the cost accounting of each department, and announced that it will be implemented from March 1st. Last night, in order to make all employees understand the value and significance of scientific management, the company convened all employees to hold a lecture. Mr. Ren Jinpin, supervisor of the company, was the main speaker. The topic was "Why Use Scientific Management?" The main idea was that today's China has three major problems: first, there is no policy for governing the country; second, there is no plan for managing business; and third, there is no method for being a person. The so-called no policy, no plan, and no method all mean letting nature take its course. Letting nature take its course is a kind of action that does not conform to scientific meaning, and can also be said to be an action without a complete purpose. Actions that do not conform to scientific meaning or have no definite purpose often fail to advance the undertaking, or if they can advance the undertaking, their progress is often very slow, or only an occasional progress, not a necessary progress, or even only see progress, but do not know the reason for the progress. If scientific management is implemented, the actions of those who govern the undertaking can become planned actions, and their actions can reach a certain purpose in accordance with the plan, and the actors can know whether their actions have obtained value and whether they have done their best and whether there are ways to increase their efforts. For example, the monthly expenditure of a certain department of the company is 300 yuan, and the profit from business income is calculated at 10%, then the monthly business must be 3,000 yuan, that is, 100 yuan of business per day, otherwise it means that the manager has failed to do his best, or the manager has indeed done his best, but there is no way to increase his business, then this department should be replaced. The so-called scientific management is not a mysterious method, but it is to make manpower, time, and material resources not be wasted without value, and if there is a waste, it must make a profit. Therefore, the business rise and fall table of each department issued by the company in the future has a red line drawn in the table. The red line is the standard line for the staff of each department to observe whether they have done their best and fulfilled their responsibilities. If the business line drawn every day cannot exceed the red line, it is a phenomenon of business loss. If each department has this phenomenon, it should immediately study the cause of this phenomenon and find ways to eliminate this cause. This is the meaning of knowing its failure, studying the cause, and seeking success. Therefore, scientific management is not a mysterious method, but it is used to encourage people to do their best and strive for success in their careers. Now, the company will hold a large-scale price reduction of inventory from today to clear the inventory and replenish new goods in preparation for the implementation of scientific management.

波蘭商業教練艦杜巴摩第號航海來滬

Polish Commercial Training Ship Dar Pomorza Sails to Shanghai

Expected to Arrive in Shanghai Within Ten Days

Our Country Has Prepared to Receive

A Polish special envoy ship, carrying a group of students from that country, is touring various countries in the Far East to practice maritime shipping. It was telegraphed to Shanghai yesterday that the ship will soon arrive in Shanghai. Shanghai, the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Wusong Merchant Marine School, will host the reception. The details are described below:

Notification to China

The Polish commercial training ship, named Dar Pomorza, has been ordered by the government to visit various countries in the Far East. The ship carries more than 40 professors and students to carry out maritime practice and ocean voyages. When the ship left Poland, it contacted our country's embassy in Poland, requesting that our government be notified in advance for verification. The Minister to Poland telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing and notified the ship's schedule and date of arrival in Shanghai so that it could be received upon arrival in Shanghai.

Date of Arrival in Shanghai

The ship carrying teachers and students departed from Poland, passed through the Mediterranean Sea, and proceeded to Shanghai. The ship stopped and visited various places along the coast to make use of tourism. Yesterday, Shanghai received instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating that the Polish commercial training ship Dar Pomorza is currently in transit. According to the specified date, it is expected to arrive in Shanghai within a week from next Sunday. The correct date will be telegraphed upon arrival in Hong Kong.

Prepare to Receive

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has agreed with the Ministry of Communications that all reception matters for the Polish commercial training ship upon its arrival in Shanghai will be handled by the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and Wusong Merchant Marine School. Wu Daming, the new president of Wusong Merchant Marine School, received instructions from the Ministry of Communications yesterday and sent a letter to Liu Hongsheng of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company for verification. At that time, Wu Daming will also lead the students of the school to visit the ship.

Drafting Procedures

Regarding the entry of the Polish ship, the visit of teachers and students to various places in Shanghai, and our reception date, etc., are currently being drafted. This matter will be handled by personnel sent by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

浙省捐税監理會今日常會

Zhejiang Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee Holds Regular Meeting Today

Zhang Shouyong and Chu Fucheng Travel to Attend

The Zhejiang Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee was established last month. The association is located at No. 40 Zhen Dong Lou in the provincial capital. According to the rules of procedure, the fourth Saturday of each month is the date of the regular meeting. The regular meeting was held at 3:00 PM on the 23rd of this month. Zhang Taoyong and Chu Fucheng, two members of the Shanghai delegation, traveled to attend today. It is learned that Mr. Chu Fucheng has a proposal, which is recorded as follows: "Proposal on the Reduction and Exemption of Surcharges and Exactions on Rural Field Taxes" (1) Reasons: The decline of rural areas in recent years is mostly due to heavy taxes and fees. The field taxes in western Zhejiang are already the heaviest in the country, and the surcharges are increasing. For each mu, the total of the regular and surcharges is more than double the regular tax in eastern Zhejiang. Recently, new names have been cleverly created to increase the mu tax and grain tax, and the people are even more distressed. If we want to revive the rural areas in this way, it is no different from pressing people with huge stones and asking children to help them stand up. How can we get it? Since the central government clearly ordered the reduction of field tax surcharges and the abolition of exactions and miscellaneous taxes last year, although this province has abolished 457 kinds of exactions and miscellaneous taxes, totaling 247,511 national currencies, and reduced field tax surcharges, excluding those that have expired, totaling 803,241 national currencies, it is still not enough to relieve the people's difficulties. If we do not reform from a large perspective, there is no hope for rural revival. The representatives of the committee deeply know that the county's finances are extremely difficult, and the undertakings cannot be abandoned. It is not appropriate to suddenly reduce income. However, the people are the foundation of the country, "If the people are not enough, who is enough?" The ancient teachings are clear. If the farmers have no ability to bear the burden, they will not be reduced. The trend of owing taxes will become more prevalent, and the government's income will still decrease. It is better to quickly set a phased reduction plan and slowly raise compensation. As for the exactions and taxes that have not been abolished, according to the representative's knowledge, there are still several aspects that have a considerable impact on the rural areas. Now, we will select the important ones from the surcharges and exactions on field taxes and propose separate reduction and exemption methods. In accordance with Article 3 of the rules of procedure of this meeting, the proposal is presented to see if it is appropriate. Please decide publicly. (2) Methods: (A) It should be requested that the provincial government stipulate two things for phased reduction: 1. Construction special donation for field tax surcharges, that is, compensation gold, an additional one yuan for each stone, and an additional one yuan for each tael of land tax, which will be reduced by two corners each year from 1935 until they are all exempted in 1939. (Explanation) The construction special donation is the heaviest of the field tax surcharges. This surcharge originated from the military special donation, which was limited to one year of collection. At that time, the people supported the national revolution and paid it with pain. When it expired, it was changed to a construction special donation and continued to be collected, which is already illegal. Moreover, since the construction surcharge has been collected, the construction special donation has been collected again, which is obviously a double tax. It should be stopped immediately. However, considering that this income has been used to offset the construction public bond fund, which is a large amount, it is difficult to raise compensation for a while, so it is set to be reduced in five years. 2. The mu donation of the security regiment should be reduced by one-third from 1935 until it is all exempted in 1937. (Explanation) The counties often set up security regiments because they have no funds and collect mu donations along with the grain. The donation rate collected is several corners to three yuan for each yuan of regular tax, which can be said to be the most severe extortion. The Department of Finance has proposed to stop collecting it. Now the borders of the province have been cleared of bandits, and the security team can be transferred back to the counties for stationing. The number of security regiments can be greatly reduced. Moreover, the counties will have remarkable achievements in training the militia by next year, and there is no need for this conscription-style security regiment, which is a waste of public funds. Therefore, it is proposed to completely stop this expense in the year after next. (B) Three things should be requested to be abolished by the provincial government immediately: 1. Eternal tenancy contract tax. (Explanation) Tenant farmers are the poorest. It is unreasonable to ask them to bear taxes. Moreover, since its establishment, it has achieved nothing. The provincial government bears the bad name of exploiting poor farmers in vain, and it actually does not help finance. It is better to abolish it quickly. 2. Business tax collected by tooth banks. (Explanation) The tooth banks in various places in the province pay the post donation. Most of the people who sell goods at the banks are farmers, and they are responsible for collecting business tax on their own products, which is equivalent to collecting tax on farmers' local products. It is not legal and causes disturbances. The Ministry of Finance's document No. 7892 has expressed it generously. It should be stopped immediately. 3. License donation for civil ships with a load of less than 100 dan. (Explanation) Shipowners mostly belong to the working class and should not be taxed. Moreover, farmers who own ships are only for loading tools and selling agricultural products. It is not a business nature at all, and they should not be forced to pay donations. However, the ship offices in various places often regard agricultural ships carrying agricultural products as business and force them to pay license donations, which often cause disputes. The provincial government should amend the ship license donation regulations to allow civil ships with a load of less than 100 dan to be exempted.

薔薇園新村擴充徵求

Rose Garden New Village Expands Solicitation

Four Banks Savings Association and Guohua Bank Act as Liaison

Those from All Walks of Life Who Order Housing Can Visit Nearby

China, or the Rose Garden New Village, the founder of the new village construction, advocates the realization of a regularized, industrialized, and artistic life. Its method is to gather outstanding members of society in one village to cooperate in establishing a new life. If it can follow this goal, it is indeed a new route for a new village movement. According to Mr. Ren Lianchang, director of the business department of the company, who talked about the recent progress of the business yesterday, the details are recorded as follows:

Residential Grade

The style and structure of the various grades of houses in the village are carefully designed by professional talents. In order to meet different needs, they are divided into five grades: A, B, C, D, and E. The forms and sizes are different, but the completeness of the equipment and the solidity of the project are the same. In addition, each grade of housing has several styles, and residents can choose a satisfactory base to build applicable housing.

Payment Method

The company is purely for social service and hopes that the benefits of the new village can be popularized to the society. Therefore, the selling price of the village's industry is based on cost and no commercial attempt is made. The ordering procedures are extremely simple, and the payment methods are designed to suit the economic capabilities of the general public. They can pay in one lump sum, or they can pay in installments based on the principle of savings and investment. Upon expiration, they will obtain ownership of the real estate.

Business Situation

The general public believes that the village's superior environment, economical and comfortable design, low production price, and simple ordering procedures are the only way to solve the problem of urban residence. Therefore, those who order housing at the company at No. 918 Aiguo Road are very enthusiastic. The first step of the village's plan, the A, B, and C grades of housing, have already been fulfilled and have already started construction. The second step of the plan, the D and E grades of housing, have also been set for two-thirds. In the autumn of social depression, the company's business can still progress step by step, which shows that the problem of urban residence is serious.

Exterior View of the Rose Garden New Village Under Construction

Increase the Number

The company believes that there are not many houses left, and the social demand should not be limited to this. It has specially opened up a piece of land originally intended for planting into residential land to increase the number of houses. The total number of houses left is 32, including 3 A-grade houses, 5 B-grade houses, 18 D-grade houses, and 6 F-grade houses. In order to avoid affecting the completion date of the new village, the company will intensify the solicitation work from today, aiming to collect enough new village residents in the shortest possible time.

Liaison Location

In order to facilitate ordering by all walks of life, the company has specially set up residential ordering liaison offices at the Sichuan Road Four Banks Savings Association General Assembly, Jing'an Temple Road North Sichuan Road Xiafei Road Branches, Beijing Road Guohua Bank General Bank, and Haige Road Xinzha Road Ba仙橋 North Sichuan Road Xiaodongmen Branches. There are more than ten liaison locations distributed throughout the city. Those from all walks of life who join the new village can contact nearby. All places have charts and printed materials for your reference.

The Empty Dream of Broad Gold and Beautiful Women: Hua Zhongchu Was Escorted to Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Two Beautiful Prostitutes Suffered Great Fright, Their Looks Withered

Confiscated Stolen Silver Dollars Amounting to 26,000 in Hong Kong

!The Joint Trial of All Suspects Will Be Held in Court Today!

According to Huadong News Agency, Hua Zhongchu, an employee of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, due to his indulgence in prostitution and depletion of his funds, shamefully stole over 40,000 silver dollars from the bank on the 12th of this month. The next morning, he, along with two prostitutes, the second and third girls from the Yinghong brothel in Xinhui Music Lane, whom he was intimate with, boarded the President Coolidge and fled Shanghai for Hong Kong. The bank discovered this and urgently telegraphed the Hong Kong police authorities to intercept them. The bank also dispatched personnel, along with police officers from this city, to Hong Kong to pursue and arrest him. Hua has now been apprehended and was escorted back to Shanghai from Hong Kong on the 17th. Yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, he arrived on the Ewo Wheel. The trial of Hua and the two prostitutes will be held in court today. Hua has lost both wealth and women, truly a vain dream of beauty and gold. The details obtained from various sources are recorded below:

Stealing Money and Taking Women, Planning to Live as a Gentleman of Leisure

Hua Zhongchu had been an employee of the bank for only a year. Hua was still young and often indulged in prostitution, becoming intimate with the second and third girls from the Yinghong brothel in Xinhui Music Lane. After a long time, his money ran out, and he could think of no solution. So, on the evening of the 12th, he stole a large sum of over 40,000 yuan. On the 13th, he purchased tickets from the Great American Company and boarded the Coolidge, leaving Shanghai for Hong Kong. The cabin he occupied was number 138. Hua's attire upon departure was very simple, with only a small leather suitcase containing over 26,000 silver dollars. He planned to kill two birds with one stone, taking the two women to Hong Kong to live as a gentleman of leisure.

The Oriole Was Behind, Gaining Without Labor

The China Agricultural and Industrial Bank discovered the theft on the morning of the 13th and immediately began an investigation, finally uncovering the truth. They urgently reported it to the police and also inquired with the Great American Company, learning the cabin number Hua occupied. Immediately, the Central Police Station telegraphed the Hong Kong Police Station, requesting them to intercept Hua upon the arrival of the Great American Wheel. At that time, Hua Zhongchu was beaming with joy, planning to transfer to a small boat to reach the city and find a residence when the wheel docked in the center of the river, thinking that since the mountains were high and the emperor was far away, he could live freely beyond the law. Little did he know that the Hong Kong Police Station had already dispatched a small boat to wait at the port's river center. When the arriving wheel docked, they rushed into cabin number 138 and indeed found one man and two women. They immediately apprehended them without labor, which was at 4:00 PM on the 15th.

The Agricultural Bank Dispatched Personnel to Guangzhou for Extradition

After discovering the theft on the 13th of this month, the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank immediately completed the investigation procedures with the city police. On the 15th at 7:00 AM, An Jianxun from the bank's general affairs department, accompanied by Zhang Minde, the chief detective of the Central Police Station, and Cai Liu, a detective from the Police Department, took a China Airlines flight to Guangzhou. They arrived at 3:30 PM and then took a train to Kowloon, and then to Hong Kong, by 8:00 PM. The Hong Kong police had already arrested Hua Zhongchu and the two prostitutes and were immediately escorting them back to Shanghai. They departed on the Ewo Wheel of Jardine Matheson, which was originally scheduled to arrive the day before, but was delayed due to fog at sea, arriving only at 7:00 AM yesterday.

The Lover Regrets, the Beauty Withers

Yesterday morning, when Hua and the two prostitutes were being escorted off the wheel, many people watched. Hua was a handsome young man, dressed in a dark Western suit, overcoat, and leather shoes, resembling a worldly gentleman. The second and third beautiful prostitutes were only twenty-nine years old, fashionably dressed, and gracefully slender. One wore a coat over a black velvet cheongsam, and the other wore a yellow short coat, high-heeled leather shoes, and carried a dancing clutch. Those who didn't know would think they were daughters of a wealthy family, unaware that they were about to become prisoners. Currently, this man and two women have been detained in the police station and will be jointly escorted to the First Special District Court of the city this morning, along with the three suspects involved in the case, for strict legal proceedings. As for the stolen silver dollars, 26,000 yuan has already been found in Hong Kong. Detective Zhang and others felt it was inconvenient to carry, so they requested the Hong Kong Police Department to telegraphically remit the funds to Shanghai, which should arrive within days. The whereabouts of the remaining ten thousand yuan are currently unknown and are being investigated.

Page 16

The Changshu Ferry Boat "Xie Mao" Was Robbed

Reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Requesting Strict Apprehension by Subordinates

The details of the robbery of the Shanghai inner river ferry boat "Xie Mao" on its return trip from Shanghai to Changshu are as follows:

The "Pingjiang" Wheel Encountered Robbers First

The "Pingjiang" small steamship of the Shanghai Gongmao Steamship Bureau, on the 28th of last month, departed from Shanghai for Changshu. While traveling near Zhangjiajing, it encountered a pirate ship that fired shots to stop the "Pingjiang" wheel from proceeding. When the "Pingjiang" wheel stopped, the pirates boarded the ship and robbed it. No passenger on the entire ship was spared, with a total of over 300 silver dollars being robbed, along with a significant amount of clothing. Although the local government and military police were notified, no arrests have been made to this day. Before one case was solved, another occurred.

The "Xie Mao" Wheel Was Also Robbed

The "Xie Mao" wheel of the Xiexing Wheel Bureau, which operates a regular route between Shanghai and Changshu, departed from Shanghai this time at 4:00 PM on the 16th, towing ships from Tongyun and Taian companies, carrying many passengers. At around 11:00 PM that night, when the ship reached the Panlonggang area of Jiading County, a roofless pirate ship suddenly approached. Each pirate wielded a handgun, jumping out of the ship and first ordering the wheel to stop. Seeing the firearms, the "Xie Mao" wheel immediately stopped, and the pirates surged aboard, robbing and looting at will.

There Were Over Ten Pirates

There were over ten bandits who boarded the ship, all speaking in mixed accents. Some wore mud hats and long gowns, while others wore Zhongshan suits. After boarding, they used their guns to prevent the crew and passengers from making any noise or unauthorized movements. Then, the pirates robbed each passenger on the entire ship one by one. Passengers inside the small wheel and on the company ships were not spared. It was said that the pirates focused on money during the robbery. They entered the ship at around 11:00 PM and left with their loot at around 12:00 PM, lasting over an hour. The pirates then boarded their original ship and fled.

Amount of Losses from the Robbery

Most of the robbery victims were passengers. A passenger named Zhang Yang and his maid were robbed of over 170 yuan in banknotes and a Fang wristwatch. Another male passenger, Guan Aoao, was robbed of 100 silver dollars. There were countless others who lost three, four, or ten yuan. The losses to the ship's office were minimal. Among the cargo, only one can of bamboo shoots was robbed. Because it was late at night and far from the police station, they had no choice but to listen to their demands and dared not resist.

Reporting the Robbery in Shanghai and Requesting Strict Apprehension

After the pirates left, the wheel inspected the losses and immediately sailed back to Shanghai instead of proceeding to Changshu. After the "Xie Mao" wheel arrived in Shanghai, the captain reported it to the Xiexing Company yesterday. At the same time, we requested the trade association to report the details of the incident to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, ordering strict pursuit and arrest of the bandits. We also requested the inner river water police to implement ship escorts to ensure the safety of inner river navigation and to protect the lives and property of passengers.

The Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society Regularly Shows Educational Films

The Rickshaw Pullers' Mutual Aid Society is established to improve the lives of rickshaw pullers and promote social harmony. This kind of undertaking is still a pioneering effort in the country. We hope that all circles will give it care so that we can fulfill our expectations. The society has already realized more than ten kinds of work, such as rickshaw pullers' children's schools, rickshaw pullers' day and night schools, dormitories, clinics, and rain shelters. The achievements are remarkable. We have printed a report on the work overview. If you want to read it, send a letter to the general association at Dongjiaxing Road with two cents of postage, and it will be sent to you. Recently, we feel that it is necessary for ordinary hard-working rickshaw pullers to regulate their spirits, so we have specially installed a moving sound film machine. We stipulate that one or two times a week, we will select and show various educational and health films so that the audience can feel interested and at the same time get a useful reference. It is said that at 7:00 PM this Sunday evening, the association will hold a regular health moving film, such as the prevention of tuberculosis and trachoma, and scenic films about entertainment. The association's doctor, Jin Fusu, will also give a lecture. This move is really a necessary work to promote civic common sense and guide the masses to enter the track, which is of great benefit to society. It is said that in the past, when film lectures were held, there was always a feeling of too few seats and too many people.

Record of the Arrest and Trial of Hua Tailor, a Wanted Murder Suspect

Hua Tailor, a native of Anhui, whose given name is Yansan, is 27 years old and works as a tailor. He used to live at No. 3 Pu'ai Fang, Zhoujiazui Road, next to Qin Maobiao, a fellow villager at No. 12, who is 29 years old. They have always been good friends. Recently, due to a money dispute, they quarreled with each other between the fourth day of the first lunar month, and then fought and dispersed. Hua Tailor then went to Minhang to stay and did not return home. At about 9:00 PM on the 14th of this month, Hua came to Shanghai to visit a friend. He happened to meet Qin on Ningwu Road, and they quarreled again. As a result of the fight, the two rolled into the nearby river. Hua managed to climb ashore, his clothes and pants all wet. He ran to Cao Fushou, a fellow villager on the road not far away, and borrowed clothes to change into. He hired a boat back to Minhang overnight. Qin, however, suffered serious injuries and swallowed a lot of water. He barely managed to get up and walked a few steps before collapsing to the ground, lying on his back. He was found by patrolman No. 2624, who sent him to the hospital, where he died. The body was taken to the corpse examination office on Feilun Road. The prosecutor sent by the First Special District Court confirmed that the death was caused by injury. The body was handed over to his wife, Qin Jiangshi, for burial. Recently, Huapu No. 1821 talked about this matter with a friend surnamed Kuai and learned about the location of Hua Tailor's hiding place. He reported it to the Yangshupu Police Station, which sent Huatan Zhang Yunjian to Minhang secretly the day before yesterday. Together with the local security team members, they arrested him, brought him back to the police station, and detained him. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court. Li Zhishan, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, explained the previous situation in detail. Then, according to Qin Jiangshi, the wife of the deceased, the defendant had borrowed three yuan from her husband, but he had not been able to get it back, which caused the disaster. According to Cao Fushou, they quarreled and fought at that place because of the money. Yu and a local named Yang separated them, but then they continued to fight. I don't know when the defendant came to my place, saying that he was pushed into the river by Qin, his clothes were soaked, and he borrowed clothes to change into and left. It was not until the next morning that he learned that Qin had died of his injuries. He presented the clothes that the defendant had changed into for inspection and requested their return. When asked, the defendant confessed that on the first month, the deceased had colluded with Cao Laowu and others to forcibly demand three yuan from him, slapped him in the face, and his friend surnamed Qin punched him twice. He did not borrow money from him, so he went to Minhang temporarily. At that time, he fell into the water in Ningwu Road during the fight, but he did not expect that he would die. The rest of his confession was evasive, asking for forgiveness. Judge Xiao Xiefen ordered him to be detained and rescheduled for further verification.

Li Jiaxiang Was Sued by His Father's Concubine

Requesting Alimony

Li Jiaxiang, a native of Hefei, Anhui, who lives at No. 7 Ruizhili, Maitehesituo Road, is a descendant of Li Hongzhang, the late Qing Dynasty Prime Minister. He owns real estate worth no less than five million in this city and Wuhu. Jiaxiang's father, Li Jingju, also passed away. However, during his lifetime, he took a woman from Yangzhou, Chen, as a concubine in Wuhu during the 32nd year of the Guangxu period. The following year, the woman gave birth to a daughter and lived in an outer room and never entered the Li family's door. Now, she is living in Shanghai, is over forty years old, and is in dire straits. She has repeatedly requested alimony from Jiaxiang, but all have been rejected. Chen recently hired lawyer Zhao Shiji to file a lawsuit against Li Jiaxiang, claiming that she is now forty-four years old and requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay her alimony of sixty yuan per month until she is sixty years old, totaling 11,880 yuan, and that the defendant pay it off at once to maintain her life. The First Special District Court has summoned the defendant for trial. Since the defendant did not appear, it was postponed until yesterday afternoon for another hearing. The defendant was still absent. Judge Qiao briefly questioned the plaintiff Li Chen and ordered another adjournment, waiting for the defendant to be summoned to the case for review.

Announcement of the Umbrella Industry Trade Union

The Shanghai Umbrella Industry Trade Union has decided that the spring and summer seasons of each year are the most prosperous times for the umbrella industry, and the affairs of the trade union are also busier. The original guild hall in Jiaxiang Pavilion is not enough for office, so we have rented No. 193 Yanhai Road inside the old North Gate as the guild hall, and we have already moved in for office. We are doing our best to rectify the guild affairs. Regarding the organizational aspect, we have stipulated that from February 23rd to March 1st, we will handle the general registration period for members in 1924. We have already notified members of each factory to register with the guild and receive the membership certificate for 1924. Regarding the outstanding cases, the amendments to the conditions of workers' treatment entrusted by the last congress of representatives, such as Article 2, each factory employing workers must employ members of the professional trade union who hold the current year's membership certificate, and non-members must not be employed. The membership fee shall be paid by the employer for the whole year. Article 3, each factory employing five workers may employ one apprentice, and so on, but those with less than five people must not employ an apprentice. The basic fee shall be borne by the employer and paid according to the workers. Article 4, the wages of workers in each factory: (A) monthly workers, tailoring and lathe workers, the minimum wage is 25 yuan per month, binding, the minimum wage is 20 yuan per month, board and lodging are provided by the factory, and the wages may be increased by 20% each year. (B) Piecework, the wage for lathe workers is two cents and two mils per umbrella with eight ribs, and three cents and three mils per umbrella with twelve ribs (silk umbrellas and embroidered umbrellas are not included in this example). The whole piecework is seven cents for each item, and board and lodging are provided by the factory. The wage for female workers is one cent and three mils per umbrella with eight ribs, and two cents per umbrella with twelve ribs (silk umbrellas and embroidered umbrellas are not included in this example), board and lodging are provided by the factory, and the thread is provided by themselves. Those who are better than this method will still follow their old methods. Article 6, the employer must subsidize the trade union's welfare fund, five yuan per car per year, etc. The ten articles have been drafted by the board of directors and reported to the party and government organs. At the same time, a public letter was sent to the Shanghai Umbrella Industry Guild, limiting them to appoint a representative within three days to discuss the matter, otherwise, if an accident occurs, the guild shall be responsible for all responsibilities.

New Contributions of the Guangji Medical Journal

The Hangzhou Guangji Medical Journal has been published for more than 20 years since its inception, and is the oldest among the national medical journals. It is published on a regular basis and has a good reputation, so its circulation is quite wide. Recently, it has been sponsored by Mr. Dai Jitao and Dr. Chu Minyi, important figures of the National Government, and new contributions are being made. Dr. Yu Yunxiu and Dr. Niu Huisheng, well-known figures in the medical community, also serve as consultants. Recently, Dr. Ruan Qiyu and Dr. Zhong Zhihe, who are responsible for editing, have compiled a special issue on tuberculosis, which is rich in content and accurate in writing. Among them are Li Fen's "The Importance of Spiritual Therapy in Tuberculosis," Fang Kan's "The Problem of Immunity to Tuberculosis," Gao Jinglang's "Overview of the Prevention and Treatment of Tuberculosis in Children in European and American Countries," Chen Changxin's "Examination of the Use of Bilateral Artificial Pneumothorax," "Indications for Surgical Treatment of Tuberculosis," Zhong Zhihe's "The Latest Treatment for Hemoptysis," "Indications for Oleothorax," "The Role of Tuberculin," "Outline of Symptoms of Tuberculosis Patients," Zhong Zhiqian's "Early Diagnosis of Exudative Pulmonary Tuberculosis," "Outline of the Life of Tuberculosis Patients," Xie Yunshou's "Pain in Patients with Pulmonary Tuberculosis," Ding Huikang's "Implementation of Pulmonary Disease Prevention," etc. The description of tuberculosis is exhaustive and is truly a valuable work and a treasure that is quite practical for patients.

Huahua Silk and Satin Company Opens Today

Huahua Silk and Satin Company on Sanma Road, Shilu, is a large-scale silk and satin company in Shanghai. It has always been known for advocating domestic silk and embracing the principle of small profits and sacrifices. Therefore, the company has been quite developed in its business over the years. This time, taking advantage of the Lunar New Year, the company sent personnel to various famous factories to search for exquisite and novel silks and satins. On the one hand, it painted the houses, renovated the storefronts, and arranged new and different decorations. It spent two weeks, supervising day and night, and it has been completed. It is scheduled to open today and hold a surprising sale to repay customers.

This semester, the Guoxue Study Group moved to the 5th floor of the Silk Industry Building on Sanma Road and is now opening research, study, and tutoring classes. The Public Works Department Decides Not to Increase Park Entrance Fees

The Board of Directors of the Public Works Department recently considered the issue of park entrance ticket prices and decided not to increase them. It is reported that a total of 66,685 annual park passes were sold last year, and the income from temporary tickets was 22,365 yuan. The operating and management costs of the park have now increased by about one time compared to 1928. However, the collection of entrance tickets is only intended to show a slight restriction and is not specifically intended to generate revenue. Therefore, the Public Works Department decided not to increase the price. In addition, the Jiaozhou Road Park is expected to be completed and opened in May of this year.

The Beauty Weekly, edited by Dr. Shi Shuanghu, a medical doctor who studied in Japan and a beauty medicine expert, is based on medicine and aesthetics. It studies how beauty makeup should be beautiful, effective, reasonable, economical, and time-saving. The purpose is pure, the materials are novel, the content is rich, the printing is exquisite, and the price is low. It is divided into beauty reviews, beauty common sense, makeup lectures, makeup guide, wrong makeup methods, history of beauty makeup, recent news from the beauty makeup industry at home and abroad, beauty anecdotes, beauty consultants, and beauty makeup method illustrations. With both text and pictures, it is really a must-read for modern ladies and new-style families. It is said that the first issue has been scheduled to be published on March 15, with three major features attached. The writers are all famous experts. Those who subscribe for half a year or a whole year before the end of April will receive a bottle of Shi's Beauty Dew or Beauty Snow. The retail price is five cents per issue, one yuan for half a year, and one yuan and eight cents for a whole year. Postage for other places is two cents extra. You can subscribe to the Beauty Weekly at the Women's Bank on Nanjing Road, Shanghai.

Yesterday's Judgement in the Case of Longhua Temple Monk Yuan Zhao Stealing and Selling Temple Property

Yuan Zhao's Testimony Was Vague; Yan Wanglong Was Ordered to Be Detained

After Abbot Xingkong of Longhua Temple took over management of the temple last year, he discovered that the temple's property had been almost entirely stolen and sold by the previous abbot, Yuan Zhao. Yuan Zhao had also colluded with Hu Su Ji to privately create a false contract for seventy-six market houses in front of the temple, falsely claiming to have borrowed tens of thousands of yuan from Hu Su Ji previously and being unable to repay it. Therefore, these houses were to be used as Hu Su Ji's rented land for building houses, with no interest on the money and no rent on the houses. The contract stipulated that the houses would be unconditionally returned to Longhua Temple as official property in the 42nd year of the Republic. Xingkong then filed a lawsuit in the civil division of the local court, requesting confirmation that the contract was invalid. The court ruled that the contract was indeed invalid. Yuan Zhao, dissatisfied with the judgment, appealed to the Jiangsu High Court, which upheld the original judgment after the trial. Xingkong then filed a criminal complaint with the local court, accusing Yuan Zhao of embezzling temple property. Meanwhile, Monk Minfeng of Hongshan Temple also filed a complaint against Yuan Zhao, accusing him of dismantling Hongshan Temple without authorization, rebuilding it into market houses for rental income, and moving all the Buddhist statues to a corner of Longhua Temple for storage. He demanded the restoration of Hongshan Temple, the return of the Buddhist statues, and their normal worship, etc. Yuan Zhao was arrested by order and interrogated by Prosecutor Li Fen, who found the evidence clear and filed a lawsuit in the criminal court. After several trials, the case remained unresolved. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. The society has paid considerable attention to this case. Because the situation is complicated, and because key witness Yan Wanglong (Yuan Zhao's nephew-in-law) has repeatedly failed to appear despite being summoned, the case has remained unresolved. Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, Judge Shao Qinzhi specially opened the Third Court for further trial. Yan Wanglong finally appeared at this time. Xingkong was represented by lawyer Pan Zhensheng in court, and Minfeng and lawyer Lu Qi arrived successively. First, there was

Yan Wanglong's Testimony

Thirty-five years old, from Ninghai, residing at No. 2, Fu'an Lane, Baiyang Lane, South Gate. Used to run a store. (Question) What is your relationship with Yuan Zhao? (Answer) No relationship, just acquainted. (Question) The official asked: Monk Minfeng said you are Yuan Zhao's nephew. (Yan Answer) No. (Question) What is the situation of the Hongshan Temple foundation? (Answer) It's my family's. The land was lent to Hongshan Temple to build the temple. (Question) What proof do you have? (Answer) None. Since the expiration of the lease in the 16th year of the Republic, my family has taken back the land. Now the property deed has been renewed twice. (Question) Is there a senior contract? (Answer) No. (Question) In whose name is it registered? (Answer) Ling Guyu. (Official) said: It is clear that this land does not belong to your family. (Answer) It is my maternal grandmother's property. Ling Guyu is my maternal grandmother's husband, who gifted it to my family. (Question) In the 16th year of the Republic, was Yuan Zhao the abbot of Hongshan Temple? (Answer) Yes. (Question) According to you, the land was taken back in the 16th year. Do you have any evidence? (Answer) No. (Question) How many houses have been built now? (Answer) Twenty-four buildings, twelve storefronts, monthly rent of thirty-two yuan. Twelve residences, monthly rent of twenty-eight yuan. (Question) Do you collect the rent? (Answer) Yes. The official ordered him to submit the property deed to the court. Yan (Answer) One is still here, and the other is mortgaged to Xinhua Bank for five thousand yuan. The official said: You should submit the property deed to the court immediately, otherwise you will be detained. Yan listened to the order and immediately looked back at his friends in the audience, asking them to bring it quickly. At this point in the interrogation, lawyer Lu Qi stood up and stated that Minfeng had now filed a private prosecution against Yan Wanglong in the criminal court, and Yan had repeatedly failed to appear despite being summoned.

Request for Detention

to prevent the risk of escape. The interrogating official ordered Minfeng to testify, stating that the land and houses of Hongshan Temple were donated by the old monk Guangjian. He requested the restoration of Hongshan Temple, the return of the Buddhist statues, and their normal worship. (Official) said: You currently reside in the Sun Temple. You monks make your home everywhere. Why must you insist on Hongshan Temple? (Answer) This temple is the result of the old monk's hard work. Now that it has been demolished by Yuan Zhao, and all the Buddhas have been scattered, my heart cannot bear it. Finally, Yuan Zhao testified that Hongshan Temple was completed around the Tongzhi period. The land price was extremely cheap at the time, so there was no formal procedure when renting the land to build the temple. (Official) said: That's right. Now that land prices have risen, such things have begun to happen. Now, how do you respond regarding Longhua Temple? Yuan Zhao (Answer) said that when I took over management of the temple, it was already empty. I worked hard as abbot for several years and resigned because I could not maintain it. (Question) Did you open the cigarette factory? (Answer) No. (Question) Why are the cigarette factory's seals and other items in your possession? (Answer) Because I have a five hundred yuan share and am dismantling the shares. (Official) said: Nonsense. If you want to dismantle shares, you should settle the accounts within the company. Why are they at your home?

Yuan Zhao Was Speechless

At this point in the interrogation, Prosecutor Li Fen stood up and gave a legal argument. The official then ordered the debate to begin. First, lawyer Lu Qi briefly stated that when the old monk was alive, several old tenants renting houses at Hongshan Temple could prove that the temple property belonged to the old monk. The newly built houses all have fire insurance. The insurance policies were copied from Yuan Zhao's possession and insured with four or five insurance companies, using Hengli Ji Hengli Company and Ling Youyuan, etc., for more than 40,000 yuan. Since it is claimed to be Yan Wanglong's family property, why are the insurance policies kept by Yuan Zhao? Who was the owner before the 16th year of the Republic? It is clearly Hongshan Temple's public property. Moreover, this property deed has always been kept by the Mo Zijing family at the South Gate. After the old monk passed away, Yuan Zhao retrieved the property deed from the Mo family. Now, he requests the restoration of Hongshan Temple to its original state and the return of the Buddhist statues. If it cannot be fully restored, then a portion must be restored to house the Buddhist statues, with the rest being rented out as before to subsidize expenses. Yuan Zhao's nephew-in-law, Yan Wanglong, is selling these houses in Fu'an Lane to someone named Wang, asking for 27,000 yuan. Wang came to inquire whether there were any disputes regarding the purchase of this property. This lawyer replied that the lawsuit had not been resolved, so there would definitely be problems.

Therefore, the Deal Fell Through

Lawyer Pan Zhensheng then stated that Yuan Zhao stole and sold more than 115 mu of Longhua Temple's property, as well as seven Buddhist scriptures and a bronze Buddha (commonly known as the Prince Buddha), said to be over two thousand years old, all of which are very valuable and can be described as a world rarity. The Prince Buddha statue has one finger pointing to the sky and one finger pointing to the earth, with a value beyond estimation. Previously, Yuan Zhao colluded with Hu Su Ji to falsely create a contract, pretending that the seventy-six bungalows in front of the temple were Hu Su Ji's rented land for building houses. Because Longhua Temple was built during the Chiwu period of the Three Kingdoms and surrounds the Wangdai River, covering more than ninety mu of land, there was usually a shortage of grain and taxes. Yuan Zhao could not steal and sell the land, so he had a novel idea and played this trick of stealing the sky and changing the day. His means of plunder were undeniably clever, etc. Landowner Lu Mingzhao testified, requesting the recovery of the stolen and sold land and its return to Longhua Temple's management, etc. The interrogating official then said to Yuan Zhao: You previously said that the owner of the Hongshan Temple foundation was surnamed Feng, and the temple foundation was taken back by the Feng family. What do you have to say now? Yuan Zhao's answer was vague. The interrogating official obtained the confession and, believing that the case was clear, declared it closed and scheduled for judgment at 2 PM on the 28th of this month. Yan Wanglong was ordered to be sent to the prosecutor's office for detention pending investigation.

Fujian Education Department Cables the Ministry of Finance Requesting Allocation of Educational Funds

The Central Government Plans to Enlighten Public Knowledge and Issues an Order to Organize a Common Sense Guidance Association

Formulating Organizational Methods and Work Outlines

To be Organized by the Party, Government, and Military Together with All Sectors

The Central Public Movement Guidance Committee, in order to enlighten the public's common sense in various provinces and cities, has specially drafted the organization and work outlines for the Public Common Sense Guidance Association, and has ordered party headquarters in various provinces and cities to follow the organization and engage in guidance. The Party Headquarters of this Special Municipality also received the above organizational outline yesterday. The original text is transcribed as follows: (1) The Public Movement Common Sense Guidance Association shall be organized by one representative from local party, military, government, police, education institutions, social welfare, and cultural organizations. The representative of the party headquarters shall be the chairman and responsible for convening meetings. (2) The representatives sent by various agencies to participate in the meeting shall be unpaid positions. The staff in the meeting shall be transferred by the participating agencies as appropriate. The office equipment and various expenses shall be borne by the party and government agencies as appropriate. (3) The Public Common Sense Guidance Association shall hold at least two meetings per month. When necessary, the chairman may convene meetings temporarily. (4) The items and procedures for public common sense guidance shall be determined by the meeting according to local conditions. The key points are tentatively set as follows: (A) Propaganda on party principles, training in gatherings, and instructions on family and child management; (B) Reports on recent important political situations at home and abroad, and interpretation of laws and regulations; (C) Imparting military knowledge, demonstrating techniques, and practicing air defense, to be carried out by military agencies as feasible; (D) Propaganda on hygiene, prevention of alarms, and maintenance of public order; (E) Guidance on improving agricultural side businesses and handicrafts, and methods of transportation, sales, and storage; (F) Instructions on commercial ethics, commodity selection, and general commerce; (G) Explanation and experiments on simple physics, chemistry, and natural phenomena; (H) Instructions on all common transportation knowledge and rules to be followed; (I) Instructions on the deeds of Chinese sages, martyrs, creators, academic masters, and special national figures; (J) Instructions on the deeds of useful people around the world. (5) The Guidance Association shall accept public inquiries on various issues, answer them in detail, and publish them as appropriate. (6) Guidance or answers on various common sense matters shall be undertaken by the relevant competent authorities at the request of the Guidance Association, and related agencies shall cooperate. (7) The Guidance Association shall announce the decided guidance programs at any time and notify the relevant public organizations separately to participate. The leading personnel of the organization shall have the responsibility to convene and participate. (8) In addition to lectures, performances, and exhibitions, entertainment should be added to attract the audience's participation. (9) Simple texts and songs of public common sense should be written in public places and important transportation locations, and time-sensitive common sense wall newspapers should be changed and posted every week in appropriate places. (10) The Guidance Association shall report its monthly work to the local party headquarters and send it to the Central Public Movement Guidance Committee for assessment, or send personnel to inspect and assist.

Deadline for Submissions at the End of This Month, Results Announced in April

The Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center's second Zhongshan Scholarship Natural Science Examination Competition, with physics as the main subject, was submitted to the Ministry of Education in May last year to notify all public and private universities with faculties of science across the country to participate. The deadline for submitting results was originally set for the end of last year. However, because only a dozen schools participated in the competition and most schools had not yet submitted, the center aimed to promote physics universally and encourage young people's interest in research. Therefore, the deadline for submissions has been extended to the end of this month, and the results will be announced at the end of April. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has instructed all universities to participate.

Ten Professors Actively Promote the Construction of a China-Based Culture

Collecting Literature as Material for Grasping Reality

Creating Forms to Solicit Opinions from People Across the Country

Offering Rewards for Essays to Seek the Effect of Collecting Ideas

After the publication of the Ten Professors' Declaration, those engaged in cultural undertakings, whether for or against it, paid considerable attention to it. Therefore, the signatories are also making extraordinary efforts to realize the declaration. It is estimated that there are three things in progress: one is collecting literature, the second is making forms, and the third is offering rewards for essays. The general situation is recorded as follows:

Collecting Literature

The ten professors who published the Ten Professors' Declaration, because there are words in the declaration about reviewing the past, grasping the present, and creating the future, must have practical actions. After exchanging opinions, it was decided to start with reviewing the past and grasping the present, especially paying attention to grasping the present. The National Revolution of the 13th year of the Republic was designated as a period. Attempts were made to collect literature from the 13th year of the Republic to the present, including all specialized works and texts discussing political, economic, social, educational, and ideological issues in general publications. For each book or article collected, its main ideas are adopted and recorded for reference, in the hope that this literature will be helpful to the future cultural construction, and Sun Hanbing and Zhang Yi are designated as the persons in charge of this work. Sun and Zhang are now actively engaged in this work.

Creating Forms

The ten professors believe that cultural construction cannot be monopolized by a few people. They should collect ideas and avoid the disadvantages of a few people's monopoly. Therefore, it was decided to create forms and solicit opinions from leaders in various fields, specialized scholars, and newspaper reporters across the country. Then, the records are made, and statistics are added to find out what kind of propositions the Chinese people advocate most for the transformation of politics, society, economy, and ideology, and to report to the Chinese people.

Initiating Essay Solicitation

Ten days after the publication of the Ten Professors' Declaration, an official of a certain institution in Shanghai and Nanjing planned to donate 500 yuan in savings to the ten professors for the purpose of soliciting essays. After investigation, it was found that this person's monthly income was only seventy or eighty yuan, but he saved ten yuan in the bank every month. Although the amount of 500 yuan is not huge, it is the crystallization of years of frugal living for this person. His will is extremely firm, so it was decided to accept this amount and formulate the following essay solicitation methods: (1) The essay award amount is set at 2,000 yuan, with the first prize being 500 yuan, the second prize being 300 yuan, the third prize being 200 yuan, the fourth and fifth prizes being 150 yuan each, the sixth to tenth prizes being 100 yuan each, and the eleventh to fifteenth prizes being 50 yuan each, totaling 2,000 yuan. (2) The topic of the essay is "How to Build a China-Based Culture." The essay should include four points: (1) the essence of culture, (2) the meaning of China-based culture, (3) the opinions of modern scholars on Chinese cultural issues, and (4) the principles and programs for building a China-based culture. (3) The essay solicitation date is from now until July 20, and the publication date is September 10. The publication is "Cultural Construction." (4) The number of words is 30,000 to 50,000. After the method was decided, the consent of Wang Shijie, Wang Yunwu, Zhu Jiahua, Chen Lifu, Chen Bulei, Guo Renyuan, Zhang Shouyong, Cai Yuanpei, and Jiang Menglin was solicited separately, and they were asked to serve as judges. The above-mentioned Zhushi has no expressed permission, so the ten professors plan to formally publish advertisements for essay solicitation in newspapers in the north and south within days.

Sectional Symposia

In addition to the above three things, the ten professors also plan to hold sectional symposia, dividing them into political, economic, and educational sections, etc., to exchange opinions separately. The first sectional symposium will be held in March, with education issues as the center of research.

The Municipal Education Bureau Schedules an Exhibition of Civic Training Achievements

To Be Held for Three Days from March 28

Revised Exhibition Methods Announced Yesterday by the Education Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau ordered municipal and registered private primary and secondary schools yesterday, stating that the bureau held the Shanghai Municipal Primary and Secondary School Civic Training Achievement Exhibition. Previously, the specified date for the event was that the schools did not have sufficient time to prepare, so an order was issued to postpone the event to the spring of the 24th year of the Republic for scheduling. Now that the exhibition has been decided to be held for three days from March 28th to 30th, all previously issued methods have also been revised. In addition to reporting to the municipal government for approval, a copy is attached for compliance.

Revised Shanghai Municipal Primary and Secondary School Civic Training Achievement Exhibition Methods: (1) In order to publicly display the achievements of civic training in various schools and to learn from each other, the Shanghai Municipal Primary and Secondary School Civic Training Achievement Exhibition will be held, and a method will be formulated to handle it. (2) The association will have one director in charge of all matters of the association, divided into two departments: affairs and storage, each with one department director; the affairs department is divided into three groups: communication, documentation, and general affairs; the storage department is divided into three groups: arrangement, management, and registration, each group with one director and several staff members. (3) The exhibition venue will be located in Wanzhu Primary School in the Jiudian area of ​​Southern Shanghai. (4) The exhibition dates are scheduled for March 28, 29, and 30, and the exhibition time is from 9 am to 4 pm every day. (5) All schools participating in the exhibition should send a copy of the list of exhibits to the Municipal Education Bureau for registration before March 15. The list can be obtained from the bureau. (6) All achievement products should be affixed with labels issued by the bureau. The labels can be obtained from the bureau after the list of exhibits is sent to the bureau. (7) The exhibits from each school should be sent to the meeting for display from 9 am two days before the opening (March 26). (8) The order of exhibits from each school should be based on the school as a unit. (9) After the exhibits from each school are sent to the meeting, the school should send personnel to distribute and display them according to the designated display location and should send personnel to be responsible for the safekeeping. (10) The evaluation of exhibits should be based on the school as a unit, and the grading method should be divided into A, B, C, and D grades. The evaluation standards will be formulated separately. (11) The exhibits from each school should be retrieved within two days after the closing of the meeting, and the safekeeping will not be responsible after the deadline. (13) These methods will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Municipal Education Bureau's Universal Education Plan

Budgeted Funding of 300,000 Yuan

To Be Implemented from June of This Month

Mayor Wu of this city attaches great importance to universal education. He previously ordered the Education Bureau to formulate a promotion plan to be implemented step by step. According to Mr. Zeng Shengzu, the third section chief of the bureau, regarding the universal education plan, the bureau decided to first investigate the number of illiterate adults in the city, and then divide them into districts and grades, and write textbooks. Students are required to read for one hour every day, fifty people per grade, graduating in six months. The city has a total of about 2,000 grades. Regarding teachers, it is planned to recruit 300 people, with a monthly salary of 30 yuan, and the top budget is estimated to be about 300,000 yuan. The above plan can be realized from June of this year.
